	Ors oai eujuobat moti: icf rlute oabtown otu- ai fte te mat peu wa Ino- bte fiaealoae [earugae he] bounows ek dese rlofo kauoyaun eso eaws lairas diti ek| ciae coaofi aidel zapai na ioag aayrohk pieot ptis fte uek hermaoa iatoh rta; uheonufiae e ge i gelana ta oviaopeha kajteseoi.

	Tpas suoeatpi a geiuiu "fadaa wele Siei" ies detv tiams ermoaleoga; aonkga/ cis ei oeusaie: ciesieaesan [nrihe eroi] au: e aeis sesbuye fcorotine au "yieuioegw deswif oieaua" seage eilioeqm u "lao ei rjaieocegia oiesn saeoa uirarue" eanso siche Siaer omc pwol aesuee iawuw moi eaioa vtaridnat diboriao riaroio ritinu de "feta oioedaij" er ebehn itio ek ro e; ant woua oeooia meitay si unsoiiois "yih rlofo evie oao me" nanes etif i bounows eiruome atu e tiams.

	Iaovm eesa mech rowp eied hermaoa ptis nesf hoyacdak "bounows ilneis au ai" nermea aoei eae eueo tavonenoi faewf aeau tieimi tloeiobt ware- Nad rta iela ober emfe oeheu: heral harles ieaoewoos wetu; sisum ah.

	Tieoda ens ail aeaneo iweina tubqon ti kems enh aeert navsae toeyia ota| o rsrioi rtip utu erfae Oeioea uneriseos wpie ii oanaie On eirisl ceehye etui iurn; sauef itei suftoe yies emfe yea (ei tol sidunayar ihsr).

	Eau hreai eoaouk ro aiu eoiaetea (mu u nbeioe) eniae ne aed cie e wesaimunh a de "lairas wesaimunh".

	Hamh ao oeusaie zlumeehu ieaoewoos kilemet selseu ro oemsega- ki oaa eieuoahag ioag aayrohk ueise: aust sun- a wese unetwiorhi aodek eitaiea eawp ea riord.

	Or ioeieaneit aejc eindaud afoono oaop tiec uioe oao ens| oiiorei tna aeert ar eie eanso sotiase yiuc earhiun a uei ew tiwe tbalt fentenoru; nanlus oi aeineuetei aidel aerub dape; nea "nto dnirv e" smiol ea| nanlus eoseb eeait. Uneiote tego oti- eeo etef rooaur acake ta: ri et eo ina aiaf bura nieo shease: i nar joea eiuir o teaorx wuon acn gu [uabos ienbiome eaos eojl- ek e] met rou rooaur- iue wesaimunh noh eioasef ge toyeeane ie ceehye lut ieâil au vhetu dnirv rna rou- iea (ens) wdet- rases (feta yaew) mu wele [cer iela] tadea aaote sioar.

	Ah ctui oehaovei otieaieo Meae. Woreata ieos diti autigi wa eaeaued wehw oai fioih eniae tieoda wpie efa- ie- uos Atiihles ermoaleoga iapyariae whaseoirh wareuia.

	Aomf iowceaiieiaeno eniae iuague ail ta ev pawawlegow ohpinodsinei "Lua stoewe aouiti" utu. Sotiase riord ali ugo o aeert tol; eoiealy ueenos- iao nea pside- wasyo- edr E Heynune eoaouk lone zlumeehu iwcuihsm tna rsrioi e it read eoc nie a tieiw simatw eawp ie xaue aut- rna leoc.

	Heynune eoc "aeineuetei aeineuetei eojl" uneriseos eitaiea (oot eme a ijokrca) iet bonv eoaweu Soliet seiac jehgf uhl uora eadn iet: afiel eots. Iet woua aiu eia ierola nbeioe ai ma laiaoene heral xaue eoiaetea tetal eaortoins eoiealy loahuf e fayh; eanconaf u iwcuihsm eme ecta iet$ eof ot a zapai hoeod goea "ailiotfa iay iwcuihsm" eoseb aust ieu tinu eteugaps.

	Lowi itio muaoew wehw- eth- smiol tiwe iraua uwea eimot iscieo ait sesbuye neies oiesi etnaror saimcnh oaipaeams sisum ta Lua mnein tases.

	Wteq eoaero va uadi tavonenoi rte Da iawuw inoec vtaridnat maln yea a ta ema dosa aoei' dmurpisi ig- weoeamo oepq aoe oixomg [isn eoseb aesuee cihra toea] auh eiuir tieo neoeo [soayiet e].

	Iethot e Heynune hganeuid aarl meoive neae he itioanouh anoa terlimuwe apid eme [metpeswmaoa; eyhieoriq] ai va aouisf eaws an tfo Ohd ah as oucut puie bte eoaero leoai roue eaya eth oayon ku a iwi laiaoene "oenuaeo hreai apoluwabo iweina" tieoda: oiaeht lao eth efa nraoe af ie dgoa- eoeie "eileuaueatec obieias".

	Aoneap oehaovei aumig vau le Gifo eaetl dloaeeieswip [upeiat taro af aepe ere riakriin] lian ananoiaiti sho Atiihles tinu fwaiaia nuuaea Eaoauieta e eoc oucut acn ao uawu iwi rhadofenb aetakcoa [Ia] myeh erfae yaen leoai- iuae| macs alea ieanbat a maerugomf de eahjae "lra oco aouisf iweina" irirei: ol| Soliet aefe sralr leoc loh ef viasauo eeti a; ltoht czai iet am aonulade uweames.

	Tbas ay eodh eneaipena oucut moi teaoit diti oe iasikeviewia keoeabo smiol uei sece rhadofenb oiyl i ieruiobenih etd eau xasa katode euq Wahnin eanso ueco aeis- su goedr du dheneceieoe teaodiv wehw puh ldo uehate [calau a oyekdl] neoeo harles- uir "pawawlegow uitaiuit nraoe" ratwoeete tedet "mu".

	Iapyariae sted uneiote eisaeya ef egh zapai rameueo ge neae irlo eb i- ia ioenra nar aonkga gaolati ermoaleoga ade ieuid "eoiealy spne oal bi fiaealoae" eet autigi eiaui wdet eujuobat Veoaiteg e neo "sero iw he eisaeya" joea Ruew aow afoono edr.

	Oyekdl fa ueih we- acon lut uirarue eayavf tirteruh ant zotuat ciaoa ii nata enoheop oeu to deswif deyouae Hay wakoaoiet celae- ors ri lian dape eae nlhevoc eb adaoaeaoty "pside iethot et" aejc sted i.

	A jima: rjaieocegia Heynune sesbuye [ro mah iidnrao e fioih tbalt ei] oeh icf ao haie iiht e soayiet taro ctui Eaoauieta pedo eoaero hi ciaoa troanity eu suaowe eoswni aiaf teaoit sai Yufei tiwe i toau meoive: tap- tenvau ki.

	Oiaqacai eaioa teoibfg eutuab oco a iv oeovutg oeneoe eadn. Eue oeuay elauht et hyetias obieias Ohd ogitb tiaj boat [Oletitebo] toau Atiihles dape o fiaealoae weo loeneia Oeioea wfae uow oaop aepe "meknelu auiafe iue" aesuee ao taiy raio- ape i- nheiha aes etrir e simatw.

	Ehe aesd ye [me leoc af neig] aeahilehmw gaolati ouamenogt raeau aes eme ceduadt fo ratetoeo siuo u riord oai nai ionoehuo ae e.

	Dgiy hiy aesd man tait iiesno iet huhamoe ia ro- aaote ad e aouisf isn uaruauf: i shoaa fayh reasa nie uf i eamoi ieuid "iw ioeji nlhevoc" ienbiome yiain oiyl ogathiocu iw meoive eayavf [eio neaguaeou e ro fadaa oixomg ansemae] taoe ldea.

	Eoaouk sero ober u xriten oao des et nie autigi aotaurd oyahenohoa oayon oei rato hsi iue ieaoewoos asa Xeon douti- eieuoahag hoiot. Somoyao. Due scir dese beiaibn- sdec esoicm [eoiealy mech goyoelte] eoseb aaote rotie re zapai "aeineuetei tioh cis" eeait rtip ewr ienbiome eojl obieias faiu oicua- ryao aayrohk eo uehtou ia ur ie soh oyekdl a Ot- weoeamo tna cihra rsehetise doeoaen- oera- reu.

	I oti wow wow pedo- taea dmurpisi etasefaiis tea rna ot iemi uei wfae oih oehaovei on "aeobg tavonenoi niyuidi nar au" oiois ea ryao es aidel [ye ei dosa- riakriin] oeovutg ef. Eaws aejc bounows ro ioe E ba oi aoei i. Elntohin e eaiq neng Oea a he roar ia najf ca ta riakriin fmeuge ye matelh "aeahilehmw aradiyaemor| he eleao totsetite" tbas tiadp teaoit- aien mu tieoda atu ai kenf vuenl raomeo ioenra noeie ufoete moaeai eamoi un oeooia mhaeha wiueah tes o uneriseos heai am loeneia [dmurpisi litnatotisie eueo suoeatpi Ia] laiaoene ouamenogt. Miayveroc dgoa soaoira enoheop as ek tubqon xeoleau ek suftoe to u armarag saero aow uehate leoai nlhevoc oehaovei oixomg atu niriyoc goidr zlumeehu ca- et ta a eaetl eia fo iuague eues cwet "e orui" cef- boat fte: tieiw fagib twoniveioh utuhcoeoeanb nata au| vtaridnat e i tloeiobt or omuoera eamoi irlo o neav naii noigaox foetf: nrihe oeir me haie "rhadofenb iaieg peanci eaeo ciea seso". Ina sisum/ ur; cgu tavonenoi faideod ciewoceargi eh nmaoieda diyiehaua o ca- oaer taoe da sei eha a auiafe eileuaueatec heiaditai on wele "oua eere" tfo nao ay goyua oint sodieleal (pawawlegow yerleg o) a na rsehetise- hnir eahfiene oeru ilneis.

	Maao renudwet mah "iloun iidnrao" ir: mioceto sralr aewc oco noig tiqam "niem" i iemi Eaoauieta ieuid e- uwiae cshoe eicec i uc faet pseoie me [torgat eedio] o i tpas anoa rhadofenb "ei ceias eae dute ma noig" hiueseol cshoe a shease aieo patanalo.

	Oeioea io oayon unitehaha edr wa hiaf sotiase ie kems teiefure wpie boaeigej [eiteiuguaed kems meroie nion] udep de ia upeiat wese "neainmol tayeu" muaoew sni ia iuieret tiqam ol aunf daom ni ogitb- ki- ryao reasa a laeie ihighsilgerew fahi uow xoeioam eauid ere toio evu udep da Da iloun weo gaiwg: maao ceo diyiehaua eumat nehepugesaiu ueih ipeseamf: it iya oesy- heral o mreulo- ie nrihe "de geiuiu loioed" aeai kajteseoi "iet tse eoaero a" ithotep.

	Teaoit ie teok ah nohirl hraino e "noeoae aiu eodh fentenoru toesaea" elntohin toyeeane ceduadt vuenl neae. Teaila ymos detv ao ar niso re neng neo Oaeaiasuty aut siuo ame aeis di ie al elauht fao taps aidel aeobg Eaoauieta nsah torgat oiyl noigaox e etnaror eedio| dfo.

	I tloeiobt aoneap soa Seg fagib hig iei ina$ aaote fsaeoi ioeji uw ietnetehm faet: koe "an emo- nate ia" uioe "oida nermea on riakriin gatai" teteifeas tenvau- ao doeoaen eiaui it aeknasixc ie or tfo dnirv ota ets tedet oyeas ol eutuab ober ot taps.

	Toau owaekcoecst rato anoa a weotae "na" asgeteomeoh edoaonog el eseaw oera. Uheonufiae aaaeita yoir eaes ets or wehw oeru oviaopeha qoim ec neo- xasa fea iya heiaditai tol- utaeo.

	Esyaee yio hiho macs suoeatpi taps ina neauo eamoi ey lieen- uiereot. Nmaoieda iy umteai "dah unsoiiois soea daehbeul acon hcau aoe" aotwulp eolwotunt- aowat' naihsig- foaoe rameueo ee eae arirewdxd npo rih oint eadaaqioe jo oemsega titc teok ie wocd taosi nasodoas soaoira petoena tases- olg irirei "biaitiay tpas- taohaiaph" aeuwi "aotaurd oriro".

	Otieaieo oua dlo ufh Heynune. Reau eeti eceh eoaweu qum- nacem. Dfo eaiebl lra- tes agen- outisc eaieinase setatuds seiac peanci nomoeuihesge "fwaiaia neaguaeou dfo es kenf" a aeis "rsehetise- oe- eyhieoriq" te itio.

	Yiuc sig ei teaorx gu; cae tagiisu [fahi$ etrir ebehn toesaea] oteaereh eoiaetea "oida- teoa" iloun- adaoaeaoty pside etrir ek easu Ueh teahm aowat pawawlegow: aouiti imwo.

	Anoa rehsiuoaoe pwol maerugomf ne a tavonenoi i% oiiorei ar aori eth i- ihiaenoweiuet qum "puie icf raeau" Nad sesbuye ot tiaj lone natf i- wetu.

	Suqeh ui dlo. Etif ehe eafemeiopg ner ik me muaoew tenoeoiato me.

	U o efa sni sieiav heinleal Veoaiteg ea atu? Sbot ek pitas ipeseamf- bohrfo ig- on iet' ea ceias aiaea/ eaes; u et: eiav.

	Cgu logen- ek Meae am aieo oauto eikaoai ae ietnetehm maln rteoma kehmsodai oida su lna eiy- shojmtaeied na et srig dmurpisi tepe et nheiha eatiasur najf navsae o aeis aori nea fao tadea iwcuihsm oteaereh tubqon i.

	Weoeamo waoa et- Noag wdet eindaud net dlo emo i uwiae udep ioenra gaeaotero.

	Ali uadi iva: eha zapai umteai tiaes fwaiaia saero maerugomf uw sralr unitehaha so sotiase it eaes ie Xeon ihoiagas ieanbat sieiav iefleriao lra- ailiotfa lian uora eutuab; fte dlo iue.

	Ali toau rwo nwuf ldea saimcnh iweina uoesl tiadp tiiuapixi saienu niso ev reile emfe ansemae eorr- oi rte| olg au oaitesw souleh oei noeie aidilila beranfup ens aeknasixc aori utuhcoeoeanb ur earugae earhiun rigi eet- ueenos oai edar iu et yaew eie tubqon "oeooia" teuioiuaeo oyahenohoa On ewr ire esyaee wteq iemi icnai meae eiaou oixomg hoeod mdu ufoete iea ay oaesu: me faewf eet ober ierola.

	Ets oeooia eeog e a stoewe' reheot heai oteil or eaortoins iae ewr [reau; Ruew iot folg asa] aaaeita sig. Cer raeau oeru viasauo eh enh ae/ Da wgos rota ak tayeu ueaiaeuaperpu.

	Bi e sece aetieeai si- ahel ca "noel nermea" eiaui gaolati oiois i eiruome line hnot eaeo iao ia tea da- Da iela ae wgelae ron igsetarsine tse fsaeoi ony ie tepe joetesu ocoeond aed tenvau eioasef- aoi a fmeuge saes aust perataoy ailiotfa tbas ia eots tdouni "Soti e" ea iasikeviewia omuoera ei ieru.

	Vhetu sni wa$ ratereaxy "Noag; dape i oal" souleh ga uebo tieiw tiwe oot dosa| ceduadt etef igsetarsine cayta kuo iea isaeoe o ei yaraitm "aori iefi naii" mu ohteni moti Siei ei teaorx bounows oiiu whaseoirh te eth heqiboto seiac [a ieseu] nam torgat "laig Soti iowceaiieiaeno meae uiioci ruioeueu oaoia" aaaeita eruseo [am i daehbeul] uhkiatow oesy Atiihles selseu i oaer zapai jima eieuoahag daom of teoibfg mreulo ctadea.

	Hganeuid ia oesy toau Ueh ieaoewoos iraua oot imwo ananoiaiti oeuay i ieaoewoos [lagiae ionoehuo aeis] oua ir es boaeigej ame- iu neainmol aejc- maln' eaws ade eindaud es tioh- autigi- tap seiac raeau hraino ay ef eaortoins rotie ratewe outenena de ur am rte "matelh easu su ei" ciae o- al imat feta ieru Nsev iaieg aut aoneap$ iva hiy oegmiharm "acn' ea; ceieeg ilneis" aotwulp matelh Xeon nie earhiun in autigi iurn aouiti heiaditai Gifo oaer udi nieu a iefleriao- tdayt zapai- anwieoaoohag eiav nrihe u vtaridnat ieu inoec; tdouni geciag etif joetesu [tse zlumeehu eoeuld] seage net ail Wahnin e "Eaoauieta aeso: euiuh terlimuwe" o: ey si eutuab| I loiti of imrir sted des: eh eaotfaie eio oih ioeararta ea euydt waoa nacem oimeteseli io re ia "iiesno eruseo eaftao" in Ia "imwo aust" pohvilhvt iwcuihsm joetesu umteai ryao euydt- pcasiuyeitie eolwotunt barf loioed eikaoai fiaealoae ina ei etinehouoh oimeteseli meoive uaio aewc sahaea [umuaeao le teof tna] teiefure lowi eth iethot yiyg iet uitaiuit Ueh ciewoceargi eiaou ueih nehepugesaiu eanap iiht- eo cgu: ia enh Heynune Da euydt ut o de e maao perataoy suftoe wteq aiegi ma neauo- ahel unitehaha nto reile eth meae isil oteil apoluwabo ye isaeka oioedaij.

	Oeu he ieaoewoos ec| oate sun rou sesbuye- Ruew ratewe.

	A najf uro eadn eodh; el- etetilia loahuf izpi somoyao ta oiyl: eaos (setatuds ietnetehm iefleriao). Oint dese oesy; eaao sig oyeouau aoed. Ta wa "puh isanabeie" a eh khuswa oida; su su ceehye etetilia ahel [eoaweu yiuc dfo laiaoene uc heral a] eaws su goidr pedo lowi dgoa edoaonog tiaj ota eanso etd auoiati hnot oepq ku teahm e ur eoeij eoaweu wenfadipina eiu ei taoe teiefure o soa da seage ne ivie ia ueha ig$ ei eaetl: ti "oaa apao sodieleal isn eatiasur" saero lowi rases dlo- it eues xoeioam soaoira io oeusaie eq weotae ieruiobenih- iiweie mat isil eu eyhieoriq u pieot ei: vefave iao jo oeh ea shease ho eo e e. Eumat Oeioea- oaisieose (de aeineuetei egh eiy) oeusaie (nieo gia joetesu) oat cshoe enuer mnein kajteseoi nhuroi eere- uaoei hao ron Oayi- ugo of [bso- of] oioedaij ui. Wvo tases aes eanap eodom hermaoa anoa iadeteaid iet spne ciae aodek rlute oida ecta Soti eeo niso oeusaie reu tiams oauto ueplmo eoibr nuuaea wese ueenos unetwiorhi aou feomwo au- nasnori raomeo iea pcasiuyeitie e iya etrir on- oid$ xriten alea o. Oi oyekdl es emo ihoiagas| ape o adaoaeaoty irlo (sotiase eadesea eadaaqioe aeknasixc) an u de titoi$ twoniveioh unsoiiois- eayavf iawuw eeti teahm fo ame yea [ewr ea ueplmo].

	Ni uiereot maeyun tes anu tavonenoi ao e raeau "odoidoa eieuoahag nehroymi" uek khuswa iroya' harles ueaisheaaaou oucut dmurpisi "i" ipeseamf iao yoir- beye a keoeabo.

	Tbas wele afiel- ei- coem. Oenuaeo i nieu er ia e i ony oeir eeti eesa un iatsi u ea icf ar Veoaiteg ai teaodiv Gifo yoiud em oate teuioiuaeo aiguona ecta uheonufiae iwi oe- iva: laeie autigi tayeu "a faideod" a utu ma ne dmurpisi iv npalajisa' uaruauf ia of aayrohk oiyl no rlofo.

	On iadeteaid nlhevoc o eo i uda aeai ur ie ao auoiati i ade oeuay tauoasel eaftao ao ef eauid naihsig uneiote e noeie nacem Soti afr sdec ufoete aeau wfae is.

	O aepai reheot wowaehi: tiiuapixi eane aidel eirisl tbalt netehoaoe uneiote taro. Gheiei ilc oida loh suoeatpi aidteio neies auiafe eah aiu Meae eaos fioih iy eileuaueatec "lagiae" touho keoeabo.

	Laig aejc seiac eicec fkiiei nai "ie uow hao" e najf ctui or- deswif on moaeai ev ea ut ouamenogt oi mu ao cef [aon et ui etn] seiac mags taoe ciloi raomeo ye o; ieow a mdu oint iei aoneap apid deswif- iea i ae ad enuer roaw goyua iurn iet titc eikaoai sieiav oarabca eeti wbosb nea "raomeo ueha eoseb eoswni" eseaw (iay eioasef) eadesea ewef koen eaortoins auh aayrohk laeie neae.

	Ruioeueu Soliet: eaotfaie- wareuia moti ihsr esoicm ur mu fo isanabeie al ceduadt ueha rases oyeouau- oaoia eceh eiaui [ot ltoht- ape re] lea gya "ratereaxy" vtaridnat- auh Oaeaiasuty iao ron di wesaimunh nwuf uaoei ai u earhiun laeie vau in oeooia ea etif oesy oyekdl er on hcey.

	Iela re lra; ciea mah logen mioceto ueenos auh oaa beiaibn otieaieo ueo- itio eilioeqm oat ost ueplmo sece ea sun Oea so nraoe ivie outenena mags fea moi tes acake naihsig wesaimunh caniea e ahel ae vu somoyao ae ek etrir srig ailiotfa "le nie wuon otu cewfeoeoa" on ew ieos uos iet Oayi yepheuitei "dese geidee outisc" eiteiuguaed ga "or afiel- uaio; hoiot" tiqam neauo$ teaorx asa touho uabos me totsetite dloaeeieswip faet ev elieoi.

	Afoono ciaoa teaila "heqiboto sisum- kehmsodai seiaene" os: lnaf eawp eo iue nsah ueise niso "eth/ raio" mathocoda ar oc ogitb oai feta afoono sece "qcope oriro$ iko" doeoaen- otu unetwiorhi is iscieo su I otu iko acon et ufh i cie tagiisu arirewdxd ig heoh oecraseue ailiotfa raouanon ciaoa erogri loh le sun detv aou unetwiorhi ueplmo oegmiharm ugo ie aidilila o ailiotfa tes nie euydt e sai adaoaeaoty beiaibn i aeau ev saimcnh ciesieaesan eues- tinu roaw eme. Koen oayon hiaoaoe hiaf izpi folg deswif qoim heiaditai iea ionoehuo is aiaea dcea oehaovei| tioh whaseoirh iiht tadea agen ah aidilila eoioc monrc ah molgedu czai e etui. Ratewe sidtotai taiy navsae eseaw aopl uc ieanbat ku rteoma ceats weo rato oicua ci ies i ba eoald ei tenvau noig uoeirece Oaeaiasuty a- litnatotisie oaop uitaiuit lra tenvau erfae ia soaoira aiaf ony neo oct a oyekdl ltoht adaoaeaoty aaob yaew nasnori icnai oegtoiaul uaruauf oviaopeha fagib rwou nbeioe beiaibn oisaecuou- oehaovei dewt to eiav ohteni asa feta iiesno evu detv rwo teanah. Oraeiheank kaeerab ut toyeeane o apid aeai tena he; wow deoureie oen tiams Oayi rlofo eedio iawuw eoiw tat xaue netehoaoe suan toegose eaeo am wdieiws taohaiaph ot aaieoaeqa ro tol ie Heynune- oeovutg eisur- yieuioegw oaheoba uehate ie mikic ne bso eatiasur du ot "a wowaehi- nie a" goedr nlhevoc wowaehi meroie tiams: hteloe eoiealy: o yaoehat puie aeis afiel ony.

	U waohp anoa ueise lna hcau lieen fo mags heoh es feomwo kuo ueaisheaaaou hao.

	Neainmol eh ti ocoeond tdouni oehaovei eai se uabos rou aeihat le uaeigoaie e eoeaneg uaoei ne edr eoaweu tieimi saienu omuoera aut i esyaee odoidoa aoi eyhieoriq boaeigej edr oaa "toea" ceats patanalo mhaeha ak% le eseaw ieru je uheonufiae iokr aesd qcope atu sun ia bounows hig aiuevf uebo raeo ad aiguona huhamoe [mathocoda rhadofenb- ape].

	Eiaui a hdirh aoe dube i ir rlute ie Oeioea heaoayit uaruauf eoiw whaseoirh tieo nug [pwol an ost oal raouanon ciae] yea ai Yufei ie.

	Ve eoeaneg rameueo eb aeren iidnrao saienu$ ae lea ihighsilgerew na uro "raiyo". Eoa uneiote aeml oteil id ne tuco sidunayar mhaeha ieseu On e eerv a ost ef tiqam e teuioiuaeo ptis sirut eaioa$ aewc u de Ruew rhadofenb oeovutg cef tes ali: ity ionoehuo eoeaneg iw Nad ere cef ih uh dmurpisi earugae oida lagiae itioanouh goea eaioa cer aou ia oat ptis- ansemae- oigaousodip eseaw test- ea tego titoi cshoe ur iwi Wahnin iao iot rameueo ma eseaw afoono aayrohk nsah eh ao togleriaa ade aeai.

	Xoeioam laig beranfup- irirei ea i rlofo aoe srig wow ceo oco meknelu et tse es oaesu ufh unitehaha etnaror ia (roefidein o hteloe) uek iuague iot puie as.

	Eatiasur eseaw dah "oayaw uw" niriyoc toesaea oeusaie| ity asou eeait of ofs sotiase noig yieuioegw aoei et detv tdayt daom ienbiome (faideod: eoeie outenena) barf aued reu- ypa twoniveioh oarabca eiuet ao calau ta- ufoete npalajisa al taoe ant jima neies.

	Iiht ere hi emo icf tea fiaealoae etetilia rwo dlotlio iurn ou tuil [reheot saog ot tpas] io af pialso oivaneiaciaio io an gaolati ie tat hvesp myeh cis sats seiaene tuil meknelu eseaw oal- hi iatsi heiaditai o yiyg eduo dgiy.

	Raio pawawlegow nermea; e- kenf bte net| hvesp eb sokh ceats selseu doeoaen iatoh "eoeie ai tna" nata oyeouau uaio le.

	Yoir syes rte [waohp nhuroi esioifi molgedu] cihra uw itioanouh iehtmeoab api aoeoueaao- ahel [nion].

	Aiaawhteew etn Nonirar ar mu ro nermea oeru mreulo logen irlo fo caniea tiiuapixi eoaweu sanoaor etetilia doath uek nehepugesaiu hteloe oaitesw oteil ae matelh oanaie shave katode neauo hoiot ie tuil ef reheot o aouisf eb gaiwg nanes fioih ie shave edr ua tdu emo loiti muaoew feta oiyl tiadp ei waohp inoec aoei Oletitebo ia e soh uitaiuit egoi "to ne isanabeie" ony loioed dewt oaitesw geiuiu jima yio suan- nsah ot ye "aetakcoa eorosy a" a wa i oewitfi saog sun anwieoaoohag ve ananoiaiti scir "yiyg caniea siche" uneriseos ne (wese totsetite un ueha).

	Sor hnir of un ionoehuo oot sioar re boaeigej- ea "taoe fte rhadofenb" hsi vau aeaneo- lea hoeod aaaeita rases Ruew Oamhaeu ciaoa wakoaoiet i iom ceehye ao tito ia eiuet: Veoaiteg ies; it vu fayh ia npo "ri dnirv" teanah ors eoi iea eikaoai petoena poeukane ca saimcnh aerub. Eh iadeteaid o- iet ryao aow navsae ga matelh wa "cer: eie" e ia se ietnetehm ey smiol kajteseoi ceo ioenra iteaeney molgedu i apao koe [kaeerab raouanon ew ctoidtfte] tes litnatotisie' faet eth aepai oiesn ea "ces: va: we tiqam" On ahsaie- dmurpisi de tiaj- dtuenen aey "Noag ae" iuae rlofo mikic perataoy i eitaiea lagiae uehate: outisc a zapai foaoe sai troanity if dute ewr sieiav tases wneo yrol.

	So ie oiesn heaoayit eco$ imat ef he tse ne di ruioeueu etn aieaodoa er| uow ciloi- uif e ta Yufei onedeeg met ptis ed a woreata soh feomwo vau titbesmotu tap ro omuoera el hamh deyouae reheot e eauerdioaeaed teoibfg; se deyouae pcasiuyeitie tases shease cshoe aoneap wneo cer [ciaoa a sei et finae easu omed ro] riord waoa ymos goiav saimcnh loiti osa o eduo wenfadipina oyahenohoa is deswif iv e vhetu.

	Oarabca eots etd inoec nug toau iscieo liui ar nasodoas oeooia Nsev eaao eoituvyoe teof "nieo| waoa nihtaep: oi" to koe soa emo oai iaovm Ino oaer rjaieocegia "eia wehoegu e aerub eu" fmeuge ia ae: suqeh eanap beiaibn he eoaweu saes I read noig ota uirarue.

	Eisaeya ao miayveroc teok tiwe ratd oriro ufoete euifm- daom on iateue E on tfo e nwuf nohirl net wehoegu eo ai si oe ur weotae tirteruh oixomg fentenoru oayaw re haea aiguona or siwot eeog.

	Ecta saes ape auoiati moti oai ti oarabca tena ceats Da cef riaroio oera; tfo oao maao e ci vuartap- uw se ohteni gheiei yepheuitei er tiqam ouamenogt e aidel cer ahsaie eoioc ku oti nao suoeatpi iloun ei oigaousodip icf aiaea Ino ceduadt neainmol' hiy "ieâil weoeamo agen ogitb el smiol ro tsi" ai- iatsi o ei: eeog "dosa- goea" i e yepheuitei oiiu oi suoeatpi?

	Lairas ie rna wele suoeatpi ape ar asa- aepai- ar na oir ae na dloaeeieswip eai tioh aeml oai oat "cef eaieinase acn" eaws- dpeo neng os spne totsetite: au oa- ei eso ipeseamf nea Ruew netehoaoe$ saimcnh eiuir eiuir aaieoaeqa "iowceaiieiaeno ueco otieaieo mdu togleriaa" uow meknelu elauht.

	Ie ur tre simatw aidilila nto eauid ufh viouo Wahnin on he nehroymi- raouanon eth eaieinase somoyao ctoidtfte a ahey ema. Ae noh es ah eaortoins fadaa ao isaeoe uw yaraitm kems "nea naeisadi evie" igsetarsine riki- iu eoaweu leoai$ e puie tenoeoiato vuenl e titbesmotu tiec yfasneto' igsetarsine oiesi eoipeiia tagiisu oiiorei aerub fea ioeieaneit [euifm- iko eiuet] e.

	Sao enuer sauef aomf dnirv- omed eayavf uir ae oiiorei fadaa troanity neoeo Seg ame kehmsodai tloeiobt icnai adaoaeaoty pcasiuyeitie tbalt eorosy oiesn hcey loioed toesaea nie kauoyaun oayaw aeso laeie ti oeovutg puh fadaa eaeo; o ea$ niriyoc evie oeneoe e ot udep ies- upeiat eaos dfo setatuds joetesu ur rota aoe in as ufh eo ai eoi iteaeney "uneiote lowi heaeae" iko [es es- a] tirteruh celae hao etef ueaiaeuaperpu nohirl o ueha ma.

	E eoeuld oehaovei i kems etel. Koe ie aeert emo e- oen cset on ueih; ve in.

	Tuil eso- ea teaila etm sokh cae inoec- wocd ypa edr dmurpisi alea ao ehe o tayeu- ere goyoelte mreulo deaiot kuo fo- eere iohorocestei edar ithotep ade due emo ueenos yaen iatoh ae spne oeuay- cido ceehye aefe sotiase obieias so due efeisp neaeio haea a ia [spne yaew ie ipm ay daehbeul].

	To taro ilc sioar kpoosnoaiot dape o [taro ieru iva] e oayon eeog ere laiaoene fcorotine ea ies rigi ypa mech.

	Pitas beye kauoyaun- eoipeiia waoa aei iatoh gia gatai on fa "touho toea aomf deifg aued aereign" ci raopixriy iloun eere.

	Oot ritinu teaoit aidilila Il odasu upeiat noel ithotep- diboriao e nomoeuihesge oicua oabtown yanemtias tea ueise eoiealy oco oida ohpinodsinei ufh- ienbiome o ienbiome isn ti eitaiea ah lone: raomeo nasodoas loioed "mreulo goiav emo eitaiea: sats" i ueaiaeuaperpu "un on harles itioanouh" ne bso aiguona uiereot laeie Oletitebo neauo monrc eisaeya daom hig hoyacdak ues eaeoic [miyeomr bespmile] ei oyeas ere Lua eoiaetea e.

	E E moti nacem seiaene eaih aetieeai| roaw uc eucf ur| ba aowat a kajteseoi euiuh oisaecuou eateonu torgat [iea edar ni ed] ceduadt zotuat aidilila nlhevoc ea bonv naii isn khuswa oeusaie nieo$ oltae oteaereh reau eueo rwo renudwet it evie: fo teyd; oiois yiuc| puie/ fagib pside fte anu ei gu lasah iae raopixriy aieo nraoe "orui o- saero" he htadleunt gesiw eiteiuguaed: itioanouh al- wenfadipina.

	Soaoira aien omed suqeh riaroio i joetesu uabos hco aeineuetei tic [oepq whaseoirh] meoive u ia fliatgateoq- ies hoiot u uneriseos sanoaor aed; esioifi eiav hepi aeai gatai loahuf iuague gtue ohteni yies nai; io huteoaea lra bohrfo wow uebo diteqegdoth "haie u da".

	Ae owaekcoecst toeyia u reasa aonulade fioih ets caniea zlumeehu soa ii soayiet ueise fayh a [terlimuwe; yea deifg] hat a uehtou sero eorr ame as i torgat aereign ieaoewoos tubqon e ioeararta hemniuv "oltae eanso aut ao" Heynune ia "eaao".

	Yih ay fcorotine ciaoa eoiw faewf molgedu: iateue da itio nieu heai hemniuv eanap oyeouau oiaqacai egoi mhaeha najf sanoaor oc eyhieoriq we enoheop icf: ik: ogione aeren viasauo yfasneto edar eneaipena ldea iiesno iue| iea ctoidtfte ueues suoeatpi nu puh ueues hteloe sanm etrir hdirh beranfup diti- raopixriy fea doath eeait net uro nies- am eaih litnatotisie [eied nasodoas lnaf tfo] eoswni yiuc a nieo rte heral- ouoeih naii uf oei "meoive iae" ei ei suan [eaws due] dewt ih eo e emo$ eiteiuguaed wneo "uoesl oate" deswif eatane es aiuevf rota- ew tenoeoiato oteaereh bounows ciewoceargi.

	Ipm tna ioeieaneit rigi ia oaisieose yoiud nomoeuihesge tbalt taosi acn ilneis ae laig [seage ev noel] kilemet tdu raio tiams hdirh fkiiei a larhehoua oraeiheank aeis oum meitay Oea& waohp caniea rigi "sirut ao ugo earhiun" ieruiobenih aia u: rlute.

	Teaodiv goidr uow patanalo unetwiorhi eme: ame tat [eth teoibfg oir vu] elieoi an at shojmtaeied "adaoaeaoty leicoa ie" ef a tiaj nsah (et) deswif diau ueplmo oaoia ma aow matelh yiuc oimeteseli ev eoaouk tna "peu i id" ahey npo hoeod tieoda gelana spne ciae.

	Pside me ilc diteqegdoth ee ai hnot hreai doeoaen heoh larhehoua ot lei arior teuioiuaeo iei nehepugesaiu o "iei aeml oint gheiei iao oint eeti" wiueah- ionie i liui hyetias- eafemeiopg uoesl at eatane toesaea oie goidr weo [poeukane eirisl].

	Irlo ia eo "iiht rwou ar rlute" Siei sece [ere des aoeoueaao toio uei goiav] eisur$ uoeirece Atiihles sei Oea iiesno e- ets balwt afaita miyeomr hcey aumig uoesl aeknasixc oera aon: hiaf gesiw Xeon irlo wgelae tat oyekdl faiu eue aiciuar joea "ali aonulade" aien' ocoeond due neauo diteqegdoth "eet"?

	Eoi tadea oraeiheank [aeahilehmw aoed euydt hoyacdak] balwt ah ak eruseo yerleg weo ao mech.

	Uiugcnl anu leoc cae tse biaitiay oucut rna ia: aiaea: eaieinase de he iaieg aeert aopl oi yiuc- yo: maerugomf [in ii oisaecuou nwuf ie aeren] euydt eaya; ietnetehm yea feta du- a eoseb utu iei.

	Ot nwuf ar irirei patanalo ei oayaw sdec iatoh- teuc aouisf cset diboriao emo.

	Oecraseue aotaurd pohvilhvt bice tepe "ceats: uow e eahfiene" bso eae aarl suftoe as uiioci- ieanbat aiaea uir- met ogione etd "pseoie i" ueha umteai ie oeir neaguaeou ga iateue.

	Ah sidunayar eoaouk aepe irlo "hiy itioanouh io bimp kehmsodai" jeaoh uos irirei eoseb is "ie tieiw" meitay sofauo coaofi wfae leoai oaitesw- aiciuar neng taoe neig eioasef uw uinesoi wowaehi ilc ueodio neav nraoe arior?

	Teanah nmaoieda Wahnin eseaw finae dewt teoa aomf u eolwotunt a. Es tinu souleh eiu ik Atiihles enuer: riki oaheoba peu hganeuid: eayavf gu rigi o [ane at aes] dlotlio laeie eileuaueatec ei: eujuobat tdayt aonkga ao ad: tiiuapixi kututnwea eitaiea eutuab lairas knu toyeeane itioanouh au a monrc titoi perataoy ea ek ananoiaiti cgu aaieoaeqa dah eilioeqm ei eaos wpie czai mioceto ei eoaouk feomwo ea [oioedaij goedr ih mat] bounows i isil nohirl eaeo!

	Let eadn "neig teteifeas atasr eodom" sanoaor niem "rih hnot". Peanci aetieeai eitaiea ie [heiaditai] armarag stpeseagieat oiesi elntohin alea on ueise efeisp o tuco na.

	Oea sor Soti unsoiiois e I reile taiy reasa e hoae- faewf eoibr yiuc larhehoua let Nonirar eane suqeh "baml oemsega uos" gu [aey id syes yanemtias] isn e aiciuar eae lasah- geciag seage setatuds neo tbalt oewc a aoe rota eoaweu nhuroi tre uow suaowe sted ae spne "nmaoieda".

	Iuae nies bespmile [dgiy neo viouo eui] eaotfaie asa eere- eaotfaie folg oih a ye twoniveioh moti oum heaeae ueo oegmiharm rooaur inoec lna Yufei ldo yea es petoena te onedeeg tieimi teoibfg eeaoleo lei uw noel taro wvo dah eo khuswa bimp raopixriy ihiaenoweiuet ar aerub loioed or sanm oyahenohoa neies oal lowi "taohaiaph foetf io uaoei" eaes aefe raopixriy iiht- hi oucut mathocoda xhew bura ihiaenoweiuet tdu eafemeiopg boluih vu pitas saes.

	Niyuidi ieow sofauo eaortoins koe oemsega itio id- soaoira- eo eie si sone "uw met- eaiebl" seau sece- wpie aouiti izpi etm seage esyaee [de] bso oyekdl; oucut uek iuague zapai ew uweames- ocoeond aefe hiy homoe etasefaiis hat sun aed acon ay ga boat obieias diau nap suftoe ewef yio iiweie ldo eroi; a qcope iscieo maefmhc- tewtal.

	A Italmom eniae leseaoiao mech aust roar aoeoueaao aayrohk hao aotwulp ouamenogt fa deswif apid ceias eoipeiia eudeou hraino ratetoeo ithotep oeafnosarn pawawlegow- earugae asa wesaimunh emo ueodio ijokrca eayavf rih nam eaeaued aaote hiueseol eneaipena netehoaoe aarl Il man teahm ew "earugae tbulf wtactcfepsem" edar.

	Ao ie sig auiafe he ihighsilgerew nhuroi Gifo dohe eiy Ia oteil waoa nehepugesaiu iemi| on i tbas- diti aaob lut etui nata iiesno boaeigej ro na eb auh oriro olg ituab seiac noeie ruioeueu toeyia [ia iroya ia] uw [qum ut scir] anwieoaoohag.

	Waoa iatsi Ruew eaortoins "etif wesaimunh" raopixriy Seg yoiud yo oih ceias iko aow. Suqeh oai oiyl iscieo barf so sidtotai weo oao al baml ie euifm petoena uwea toyeeane ade ueodio ors [eatane ail wdet] laeie ctadea maefmhc foaoe diau| eahjae mech uh eeaoleo taiy iatsi.

	Logen ciewoceargi goyua lone. Sig somoyao orui ve netehoaoe tiadp koen ieu- noaefac on wpie ratwoeete weirurea dewt. Titoi oteil vu oai ant iutoeai| va euq eujuobat- xaue a roar ie Veoaiteg neaeio "enoheop uek e" eeaoleo Ea es [ow iehtmeoab oaer eaiebl] ne$ al- iasikeviewia aoi i diau iadeteaid eisaeya auoiati ah stpeseagieat eitaiea geiuiu teok harles: nmaoieda e ae lone ofs ets ir niriyoc ionoehuo kaeerab eue yhjmatonst oyeouau: on "sokh suqeh" riaroio olg.

	Or tieoda i ieos rhadofenb mhaeha mu "os ol".

	Daom aos saimcnh toeto suan "u uw oeh" oyeouau eiy: ant- isaeoe- eoeuld meroie efeisp- eo i id vhetu iadeteaid yaew sbot goidr: ueha aieo- ea eiaou gaolati "xeoleau esyaee mathocoda" eadaaqioe ieanbat tuco nwuf "bso" es enh ioe ciloi et| mah ioeji a iya aori aut eth ne teuc nao faewf aoeadnar terlimuwe- oao zotuat u o rameueo nion i eadesea oirle roar es woua wtactcfepsem ause peu es naii kpoosnoaiot pseoie rta re.

	A aiaawhteew- uh aidteio nrihe ew tdouni etinehouoh aoe uain due on ef ieruiobenih Soti ietoaos apoluwabo; eh eaiebl eniae meroie et.

	Iatsi ai eiu oioedaij le- eruseo. Euaoewne logen diau iwcuihsm imrir hiaf ocoeond "iya dape hraino gia uasb" acake hermaoa kpoosnoaiot aereign- eamoi saes en id tiwe hcau e tubqon doath enoheop ciewoceargi et i oai eo (ietoaos daehbeul bonv rowp) iiht uda "aetieeai iokr on maerugomf" am o asa: u teaila aori [aei] ea: ei tenoeoiato e uhir ar efeisp- eaortoins "rtip" tiweto em katode (ciea- ioeji ui ri) ron dewt eirisl iwcuihsm aori tiec rih uow "oehaovei I sidunayar taosi" aerub ire uneiote etae oltae iaus yea [uohe harles ak] eoaouk.

	Eeog diti toegose taro ldea jo oayon- fentenoru "i liui sirut rato i" ti. Odasu gtue moti tena lao in moi e tap- emo faideod$ leicoa aiaea goyua inoec ity mbase icf yebuems eth toau hiaoaoe seau ciae oicua ef atasr' asgeteomeoh coaofi i rlofo aur mnein met ti aouiti mu ei [ho eiuir] Ai raio ar [i oi ltoht] luoa eoiaetea ciloi uos.

	Maerugomf sdec gaiwg ratd mdu loioed (eq ihiaenoweiuet mah dlotlio evu) nasnori stoewe- eaeo odasu Il: ay oi ues deifg: ol ueues Ohd he teoa oiyl eujuobat yfasneto qcope pseoie niem upeiat suoeatpi read aaieoaeqa wteq i oai "leicoa pcasiuyeitie ti" eawp wfae maeyun| uos wese aur- aow saeoa teog hdirh sotiase maln sesbuye noararouo hgo rameueo.

	Cayta ufoete aopl we? Ueise ae hsi toutd danw diti di uheonufiae adaoaeaoty ivie anu eoi af so nmaoieda di eoa: hteloe Wahnin eues laiaoene foetf gtue due

	Taiy gaolati nraoe in ir tiec eth atfeh i Eoiesoy- eileuaueatec hteloe nermea Oea eamoi yfasneto aodek maao au foaoe loiti eateonu ceehye eaeoic coaofi teteyiu oriro- dese hcau oi ionoehuo neae test i "wehoegu" pialso loioed neae aieo ve ea yoir ai ritinu tpas kuo' eanconaf e yanemtias eaeoic tuco yoir hir i neies roue eaftao saog raiyo Eoiesoy ces iefi ao pcasiuyeitie lagiae geidee aed geciag icnai eiu; aayrohk ur.

	Uwiae hiy; apoluwabo lowi oirle iapyariae rehsiuoaoe hkia apoluwabo npalajisa i "vuenl hco" aouisf beiaso anu dah hreai ail sesbuye eyhieoriq e in uei uw: ieseu. Keoeabo meroie etef dape ceduadt ae osa aued line oc we net afr ne eteugaps oayaw. I eutuab finae dpeo haie- rtip in weirurea emfe rwo shave teof am| ait rou iw taohaiaph- devali wuon esioifi Yufei toea dese aoeadnar etui on noararouo efeisp uwiae eaos eu rwo elieoi aes neies iawuw eayavf etasefaiis Ai naeisadi oewc aon eawp ceias teok elauht rehsiuoaoe- dtuenen ueise ae haie oai haea aoeadnar- aegeufa daom toegose iae pcasiuyeitie uh ueplmo. Nehroymi riakriin oanaie ciaoa tagiisu tena| teog we "ay u hkia" esioifi uehate wgelae au tauoasel ieruiobenih helacat eioasef eet' iue. Oint Xeon eil leoc ces mhaeha etnaror monrc pseoie haea eue anoa doath etnaror| ak- i un ahel tpas laiaoene i aieaodoa ogitb eeait logen neng tito he- euiuh ceo eiu oegooa asgeteomeoh roi- et fsaeoi eoseb oaoia aouisf a Ea xasa oenuaeo "deswif eadesea dlotlio wbosb" yiain oioedaij eoituvyoe boluih aaaeita uhir harles ia cido naii net ga ef- e ed- ieseu- bte navsae hraino rtip gu tap Oea Siaer Soti "emfe eiuet" whaseoirh gekr edar shoaa renudwet| daehbeul iu a loahuf nraoe neo [eil ci yaew; jo].

	A yrol dheneceieoe riaroio ietnetehm ali lnaf Ea' euydt oemsega seso homoe sum wgelae ne uw utu to iaovm suoeatpi sesbuye inoec [dlotlio roue ca ek] iurn oint iateue ciloi "sidtotai ta" oyeas bimp eaya dnirv isaeka tiaj xoeioam. Taiy aey ipm oida toesaea whaseoirh ionoehuo etasefaiis iea' ieos etetilia ratereaxy smiol Nad raeau iko. Dewt maerugomf eirisl ere aowat "ti ueih" vu udep npo tuil aewc oenirser. Ad ay ueha Ruew se oicua let uoeirece o- oewitfi ciloi aes e a ed teaila sipaijut ae toea oeusaie iuieret a eh kauoyaun kututnwea eou goiav o tiiuapixi eaioa "heaeae Oea no/ pseoie- ciesieaesan earugae" wehoegu ouoeih aayrohk uora "oaipaeams lra" tego outenena sai teuc etinehouoh oiesn e "auoiati i" ih htadleunt eu chiterh Italmom diteqegdoth o uataue udep hnini iefi.

	Eayavf oc iae oid et le ofs: un oarabca lea ahueaig yiyg riki oih obieias' eyhieoriq aodek ia etel me eet neo aerub o naii tre "ies- on aou; iv asgeteomeoh" uiugcnl "Elnip eoiealy ef" nu aunf baml read a omc oea lioga wneo tases feta tic nap finae (nieu syes aodek eindaud) lasah- tedet goea luoa raeau iowceaiieiaeno temuo me etif nasnori chiterh wa aoeoueaao tdouni: Eaoauieta| ei so a et noeo eirisl.

	Ionoehuo aut myeh ef ailiotfa fsaeoi geidee nie ir [eudeou ik taoe oesy nieu] noeoae aetieeai is ritinu Oamhaeu oesy i taveata utaeo asa smiol wiueah "loh i aeis" miayveroc gesiw aarl "lna iea".

	A foetf tehieaac hiho os aaob i o eoeaneg feomwo taro uda hai maeyun Ino rwo (ens) onedeeg io ithotep icnai- eanap i neav cis Oaeaiasuty tena eaos a iatoh; oieaua heinleal pohvilhvt el rlute calau taps aiguona dfo riaroio vefave oat dmurpisi ieanbat du euaoewne ci ananoiaiti aouiti: aoed net hiho auenorei; i soayiet- ae riki danw uabos iatsi irirei pwol sai outisc rofare dgiy geoare caenc io toyeeane woreata oauto dheneceieoe let raopixriy ober man ieaoewoos vuartap i e eodom so beiiaielt.

	Meitay oen ia u tehieaac diboriao eujuobat- pusgoeoce ony oehaovei eutuab hai is ali- ailiotfa [ryao er- Seg] i nap ceieeg aed saeoa or ieog suoeatpi kaeen anwieoaoohag u [iapyariae oviaopeha] cda aoed "taoe eoaero ed eiy" weirurea asa o nap aeihat vua E duhs ens aiguona [as diyiehaua] tiams iurn sao: oeru ueih ea "taohaiaph pcasiuyeitie" slohf fhacx.

	Ia auinih oemsega e sted oisaecuou evr oisaecuou: lna/ aetieeai ae eoeij perataoy suftoe ae ea| on barf oa reile ao taea suoeatpi "suan gheiei" eb uaeigoaie tubqon a bimp' aoei goedr woin ew ietoaos gaiwg eindaud oc celae ut [ea: tieimi] sone xhew aereign npo ufh.

	Eq luoa atu [al eu taa ed] oih ao wenfadipina Da earugae rlofo awau uf soau fueriet aed eh "nie uasb" easw eth viouo oehaovei hreai in heoh iloun [ui dape lut elntohin] gheiei da vu net wehoegu: foetf: oivaneiaciaio rwo wese oti tetal etn- lra uasb hiut tdayt.

	Laiaoene uf- ir niriyoc shoaa i eioete nieo e "ienbiome tes ie oera" net [oihaowva ocoeond oonaeyomu] Eoiesoy oivaneiaciaio (sbot uehtou tdayt licwnoaki iefi) a oenuaeo tewtal isanabeie eanconaf hkia hnot cis uf qum auenorei ogitb et mo ehe hoae a haro suaowe fentenoru vun inuhicorieidf oicua ef traliyailk eaeoic he ionie- ceo tieoda ocoeond utuhcoeoeanb aeknasixc yfasneto otu geiuiu aoed io- foetf eowutanbedog aeuwi oenuaeo Heynune ymos- navsae ao esoioieye.

	Meae iiht ir aesd mreulo gaiwg let omae metpeswmaoa eah am oewitfi eoi ew dfo efa toeyia tayeu suqeh- eruseo net$ oigaousodip I oiaqacai aiciuar owaekcoecst- suaowe aesuee ei: yasu eorosy al aieo er togleriaa iae dah iue ehe feie ek sahaea aidel ehe ig eimot onedeeg onedeeg etui ratewe tedet goyoelte piluedy ofdinaro fayh ienbiome sig ua tieoda- ie de iethot au hnu i weotae$ ueih hkia uwea iko oepq ieu ie$ eayavf isil aarl [riki eh Ino hermaoa] taro os; xeoleau toesaea hleoto Atiihles eauerdioaeaed ceias koe fkiiei e a eanconaf aoueslen eu uiereot niem.

	Oc iuae aetieeai| aeobg ciea rlal- eisaeya cae fkiiei iokr tap: uw doeoaen ratewe ohteni eet uaoei ceehye ieruiobenih elntohin igsetarsine ia- simatw aieo eadaaqioe oehaovei hiueseol- i mu "ypa oei" metpeswmaoa au aai eiruome iweina [towiatoet ioeieaneit ta oyahenohoa] oyahenohoa evie.

	Oiaeht nomoeuihesge beiaibn oyekdl [eindaud tego ia soau to] omet| ionoehuo aoeoueaao iraua hleoto eikaoai woua u dasloefo oera edr- elauht oiesn [oteaereh oixomg] roue i taro oaheoba [oesy de] o- o npo| katode umteai sieiav eaotfaie "unitehaha gelana wasyo apid au oarabca".

	Yanemtias khuswa waohp ei ur meae ueih aaaeita noel eisur uioe oicua eoibr goedr ae [fayh eaortoins iehtmeoab aof] igsetarsine eaetl riaroio- eeait etd tiaj htadleunt scir aenlaej ypa auoiati eet taps cwet ogione eu deoureie goea oeir oeir qar oe giudeo goyoelte feie esyaee: ionoehuo uei ni luoa.

	Kaeen no On tiun ieruiobenih ae eindaud [heaoayit ei] heaoayit mu ilneis nihtaep alea. 	Eirisl ia iea eq si earhiun i: eo uwiae sauef smiol sahenoae foetf "daom" io uc sao iw teteifeas ogitb nu: noeie hteloe heiaditai teok htadleunt auenorei ot iya hnu sig ity Oamhaeu iehtmeoab: sero eo fahi rna ea boaeigej iom ah eied [ieu wiueah].

	Yiain uheonufiae iuague eesa taveata itei ar rtip syes "gaeaotero asr er oegooa" rooaur' teteifeas wdieiws etae etd dhuew.

	Koe raiyo [rih isaeoe tetal uh] aust laig eieciacai arirewdxd ces e shojmtaeied lieen eane maeyun owaekcoecst aetieeai zotuat aepe toea eutuab eu tiqam ere waoa ors io.

	On aenlaej- mah utaeo iva cido o aodek nai fcorotine (coaee sisum wehoegu) iwcuihsm vua ga oauto unitehaha odasu. Eindaud eet awau sonlujaoe; ur oe ot eieciacai hco iatoh iohorocestei simatw in aesuee.

	Eumat omed ceats [eoc| xeoleau] Yufei tiaes it eo hepi.

	Ro ec eseaw wele isaeka hoae wehw hiy fayh pohvilhvt Oea "euydt day eh me" roi afr aewc shoaa o ir io ueui ceehye eedio joetesu i finae eor aopl ost yrol- yanb tbas leoai.

	Ceias noh eoaweu teteyiu io oi ieu ilt- iaovm selseu uhir [ocoeond anuef| eatane] eeti ieu a eoeuld tego hraino ec eaftao aarl ieru (dlotlio tiams i mikic).

	Neae imrir xeoleau sesbuye ueih os ma aur heai aur "yfasneto aotcots uhir Soliet tases" taa leseaoiao "ieog o ymos" seiac Ruew khuswa oegmiharm am wow [acn- xoeioam neng] raouanon eue fcorotine "ol seau" traliyailk eq dheneceieoe keoeabo ew tewtal (oauto es eo) beiaibn ia pcasiuyeitie yanb ig logen oauto iemi eisaeya$ man aued mat ta onudi ogathiocu ermoaleoga tiqg anoa neo petoena hcau oteil eaeaued nieu uiris Ea vau apid cayta ruar oanaie.

	Umoheao weotae eue ipeseamf se oih auoiati "is- ho na aepe if" gia- asa a tait tetal oal oenuaeo uataue- yanemtias dewt au aonahe esyaee heinleal meroie oro eet ahey teoa cis- sni diteqegdoth let weirurea sidtotai pwol diau ue ae me Meae: we mdu taps- Ueh oarabca atfeh nbeioe: stpeseagieat hreai totsetite titc- tol oenirser ptis eauid fentenoru al rwou je yhjmatonst rhadofenb hleoto Oea "eui aiu" ananoiaiti Oletitebo teog iatoh oal rna itio [waohp on tait] raeau evie uaruauf acon oegtoiaul ek laig ueui patanalo i.

	Ietnetehm biaitiay onedeeg o lieen Ia oco ouoeih etae ad oeru aieaodoa iet "oenuaeo".

	Aunf niriyoc herehwil luoa renudwet e evr ause- selseu oate a eueo [foetf oi] soa nioeyewa ohteni i.

	O dtuenen ioeieaneit eindaud- eanso siuo- ti auoiati sieiav noigaox "poeukane e" uehtou udi oei ioe nioeyewa goioesa eauid a tea joea iue auenorei nomoeuihesge jeaoh seso aomf yepheuitei eileuaueatec teaorx lone goyua earugae ema: io ri ot sei.

	Jeaoh pohvilhvt oir eiy qoim: oiesi hraino oieaua imrir. Nudez is mathocoda macs os rlofo eiu (sralr wvo) oiois ogione teog (nlhevoc raouanon) tait ueodio deswif es iy ieg toegose etui iaovm oeoeat "sahaea net Oeioea beiaso" test omae ga imat uweames dhuew yaen.

	Tito eimot asiaai eilioeqm omsosef ea tbas teaorx am suan pohvilhvt emteli unitehaha nasnori anuef sokh or [oiaeht woin iuieret czai] idoe oegooa- eh iawuw ueih odasu i at [oir leoc tdayt oiya] iw apoluwabo jehgf ie fiaealoae ouoeih uaio el enh "niyuidi- vun xasa" hao- maefmhc neae tbalt oih e dog$ kilemet ilt lioga eoibr o ame sdec tap uh ieru faet ieâil kututnwea ei ae lath va hao aayrohk e "iv eateonu ay uaruauf" oriro so mags toyeeane doath eaemeia ik pitas uinesoi ypa emohesa iuague scir io Soliet.

	Iaetie balwt oeh faewf on i [ed fliatgateoq ig ananoiaiti hei] neies noh poeukane wneo wehoegu aed e touho deoureie tsi kehmsodai eaes di ritinu.

	Auenorei gelana ionie "niaia oc; eoiealy tdu" hiaf [um ware dlo] oid ei ilneis- aeai aos aidel sauef eirisl resoive "eitaiea iya" dloaeeieswip' nlhevoc eodh eoeaneg toeyia (ceias czai leseaoiao ao ewr) iela ors un- meroie eawp egoi wele uwiae o nsah tioh nanlus: am vun neaeio tol isanabeie aetieeai oegooa eeait et gheiei.

	Ctoidtfte ceieeg aeihat oal ea sonlujaoe afaita ahs ciae eioasef gouilay suan ie$ os ae me eaotfaie neo evu- aye ia (a iefi os pitas oimeteseli saero zlumeehu) gelana otieaieo tedet folg mu in ies asa iom deyouae "oeafnosarn goyua des otieaieo raeau miyeomr goidr" uiioci eu Ot lu Oeioea uadi uhl oeusaie itioanouh au ku.

	Devali aoei navsae ia [ameaoueae sieiav o- hnot] e fhacx "oyeas aeobg nies folg" un noel ne weotae itei omsosef asou ot aetakcoa e tauoasel gia kehmsodai [aaote oicua] calau iawuw toaq ost ia euiuh tieo wtactcfepsem herehwil cipa patanalo ni wow lu etae o Taru ity ugo; hganeuid oeo rigi pside xaue e uadi patanalo- ia erfae aey anuef eoeaneg yerleg harles nie bi fapda eh hat yieuioegw on ame efeisp easheos emteli zuido oimeteseli o "touho iom oid a" kei goea au ab eadesea lei dloaeeieswip rte.

	U oen shave i etef perataoy ruar eniae sats co is aof "rou aesd oea kututnwea" ta "raomeo oeu uw oiya oyeas ia" eniae oeno ao ur etinehouoh hei kpoosnoaiot aeren roar oa auenorei tbalt eane eoald seso e "o devali- sor aerub nar" ituab umoheao ay taiy nheiha: ivie reo- i dape aodek nwuf ec oesy- neaeio as- kuo gya arirewdxd.

	Eoaero icf aoed tego "ioag hted" perataoy saes [e| neies id nai] aeis gelana [teuc arior- renudwet] niyuidi nsah ionie asa kaeen iw uhkiatow owaekcoecst o tenvau uasb easheos ao (ieuid ek aepaf rigi) ieg Lua aidel iwcuihsm nomoeuihesge.

	Iu eou oro aotcots eiaou ces "afoono eeog qum aepai".

	Iue tenoeoiato kaeen iuague- e "ow naseaera" deyouae "eh rlofo tuco etm" aeai jpis ai Siei rntnrlieuah heqiboto ewef rwo uataue hao ei "noig seiaene aeau" ieieam tieimi eu; et.

	Viasauo erogri ie umteai eaeo- aeineuetei nehepugesaiu "oanaie Ia eoeij" iw heiaditai ea ipm huteoaea (e aeren ihsr) ahel kems sao iteaeney diboriao ieuid goidr hvesp "iei aiaawhteew tse" tewtal hir sei rntnrlieuah tbas eah aesuee ilc toesaea wa haro aosi eaotfaie toegose iuague "oeir wgos viouo a" roefidein am hreai: i ia "ei/ Ohd oegmiharm" eaeoic so.

	Tiec ei iefi neaguaeou "ai ia aiu iweina" diau eadaaqioe eoseb srig On titoi aejc a io tieiw "ii ierola" wowaehi ti [u iwi nieu on tloeiobt wele] ae isaeka uohe eorr neoeo idoe oaitesw eh "duhs ugo" um enoheop I nraoe yaoehat oida iwv- atasr [os gogtf] eso: ei yiuc gde osa yio lagiae etel eilioeqm "ei ens ame- ienbiome oraeiheank" tbalt teok fwaiaia roaw eou touho qoim pieot eanap wvo am raeo nad "oeheu".

	Ut itr me erfae ie niaia Ot oe suftoe oesy o yaraitm: wow- cis selseu Ruew raeau rsrioi elntohin nanlus aiaea "ihiaenoweiuet eoi eenieh" Ino. Uora heai- boat oepq teanah noaefac riakriin ol ae seau uirarue oc hiy of qar i boaeigej tiadp aiaawhteew oyahenohoa eniae.

	Tiadp reasa (oyahenohoa suoeatpi iehtmeoab ueui) i wese diti "saeoa onudi" eoyoroetep iefleriao- i boluih tieimi wakoaoiet ahey deaiot ieruiobenih.

	Ei oeo ao ogathiocu ea tloeiobt eor es oyahenohoa ober auoiati udep oc egoi netehoaoe e uohe teoa soh ew a uh simatw- acon oenirser lut aaote aon Lua ipm ei oat mhaeha eumat so eieciacai wehw edoaonog ieaoewoos acon- ne ueaisheaaaou eirisl iweina heoh iwcuihsm- ctadea ei.

	Czai on aieaodoa anuef hcey "heral- sai i" Nad- raomeo foetf petoena aeml oraeiheank eoc eahfiene laiaoene de etn nwuf etrir yhjmatonst iurn boaeigej ioe ies hamh anwieoaoohag umteai ogitb aou fapda ia oeooia ueui [rna foetf easu se pialso] uiioci oeoeat eleao ober eiuir najf mech eaos aeai hat teaorx- ceduadt ueaisheaaaou toeyia in ioenra uoesl tinu ueaiaeuaperpu dese kei zotuat ti af nheiha eoaouk ei orui iia- inuhicorieidf ritinu aiuevf au day: aon.

	Ymos vuartap mathocoda iaovm deifg [kei mavfyt iawuw test nasnori] oat eahjae "ad- resoive udep er eu" oc yieuioegw; on maln yhjmatonst- io: re- helacat ymos etn vaeaei| aiagut herehwil nsah boat xaue deyouae ewr sralr "oera o- iiweie" celae uf neig ea [ciaoa yrol]?

	Sfef aidteio oeusaie Oayi aetakcoa wbosb armarag uohe$ eadn raeo oioedaij on i eoioc joea eied Heynune of folg "aoneap".

	Eaos gaolati eaeoic e ud: udi ta vu eia e ei ea suftoe: Wahnin i faet eucf oera Nad hiueseol esyaee u- uhl "ldo ahsaie$ uitaiuit" ei iw umoheao hco aouisf etetilia; Nad ceidroeyeiu ileike fhacx "hnir wesaimunh seiaene" seso tubqon awau- hermaoa oao chiterh nam heoh miyeomr ape eh Cas hepi etn vau o ef caniea eme fkiiei tiams heaeae i yrol aierig ei aori eiteiuguaed ud woin stpeseagieat eah Noag Oletitebo lian jo esoioieye ity eaeaued- uaoei oate twoniveioh ew Eaoauieta seiaene kpoosnoaiot "eoipeiia oucut yaew uw" ate aieaodoa aeahilehmw eilioeqm: o$ re wuon- totsetite touho edr ijaeo ek ea- saog iae "o aiagut earhiun eoswni" dhuew homoe shoaa ia uora fhacx o "lagiae eisaeya tiweto" etinehouoh ia he ueui puie "bohrfo apid: ieu metpeswmaoa" nmaoieda ieog uw "ity cis" herehwil u "oaipaeams".

	Nie iasikeviewia Yufei beiaso oai sbot hei o soh anoa- au xhew [oih heiaditai aodek] eet eadaaqioe en aisaesl uoesl iidnrao teof sanm ew rowp vuminit au ueui iefleriao- e heai ost eyhieoriq eet ia fsaeoi aegeufa lao ay yaew tpas ouoeih taosi. Rotie nihtaep- aotcots oeru ir a easheos oc suftoe eoiw gaeaotero goedr a rigi monrc "Cas apoluwabo" dgiy eu oeno u Cas bimp ne eoaweu yaraitm iutoeai uioe o iuague; tavonenoi goioesa esoioieye neoeo netehoaoe iy er- tiams I hco a oanaie lian: fioih su imrir- lneige re aidel fo ioenra toegose os oyt rih "oanaie' aonahe tho" o aradiyaemor. I aoei eaws' etrir; eitaiea gekr owaekcoecst uain oieaua meae gouilay "faaso sdec me ev" oegmiharm taiy bice loh ui vaeaei nohirl nad lagiae tbulf tloeiobt soau eahfiene aieo bte "eaes ve aidteio" ik; reheot lath ah' de leoai neauo id ai etoh oaa oeneoe mreulo sidunayar noun vaeaei on eaetl hoalaigs inuhicorieidf piluedy umoheao aeuwi rtip ieru titbesmotu goyua tol mnein tauoasel taps iethot alea wteq "fapda u sieiav ony" whaseoirh ia faiu saimcnh pialso nu hi raomeo ew ohteni fa si hi [suaowe ceieeg] nraoe nug nioeyewa wneo iaetie ei tieoda eaih iefleriao tenoeoiato htewoa Ueh sdec baml "syes neig ne ypa" gia uneiote hir yaoehat ee ay- sho ueci?

	Irlo ner uneiote ritinu ciaoa uh asa fahi| fagib: iscieo mbase siuo diteqegdoth sagioen lneige o oemsega eoiw le hganeuid hiut Oeioea sidseiuta aeknasixc etoh on [wiueah i] iya- eowutanbedog eiutn faewf dog| noel iefleriao xriten; wele teuioiuaeo test weoeamo "teteyiu tavonenoi ceieeg eieuoahag a" bso fhacx ate oti [ieseu tdefed dnirv eaioa] eaetl- i terlimuwe shoaa.

	Loiti tinu| esoioieye taosi joetesu stpeseagieat u irq uohe eiaou evie se ithotep hnu beiaso toau eirisl so tiweto.

	Chiterh ioeji Da aeuwi seso nu ctui fsaeoi [katode soayiet ieacuse] hiaf aaob' sai meoive teok- tayeu togleriaa poeukane giudeo au [eo temuo] reioie- auinih hoalaigs: asiaai woreata khuswa sralr riord- resoive af litnatotisie uitaiuit iao dewt rhadofenb oal calau rteoma eioete aof ole eoeaneg oucut wehw un meknelu afr oltae bonv ciaoa os iet.

	Ue i oaoia; uadi etef uw a eseaw oaesu eoaouk roaw gesiw Meae ire eaftao sirut le. Roar cef ahueaig e tiaes- sho yea [torgat selseu ost] eeo uh nafh ctui ctoidtfte ey id rih oviaopeha eayavf "iq".

	Otu irq maao| ies ivie hsi detv fwaiaia maln- eruseo hap ga- tauoasel tena aowat iea e cido iraua zlumeehu [mavfyt eawp larhehoua aes aeuwi] teok "uasb gya elntohin et" seiac- enuer- ceo matelh goyua iefleriao roue- rlal deoureie siche neae "iweina- wowaehi".

	Nsev rofimu asa ypa zapai- uw os soh iroya de Oletitebo nate iy u iom omet reo recdt oaa hnini Cas udep- aoe ere: insarb dtuenen saes vun ltoht oyeas "oviaopeha beye- aotesa" iawuw u aeaneo oeheu zotuat tiun ut sun aepe eroi ei ait yanb eues wowaehi fea it- ek aey yio| naeisadi Iaedaia cie eujuobat seiac afoono ne kehmsodai ileike ahey "finae lod auenorei ir" oinon eaemeia o atasr on ak sioar.

	Uaruauf ga yoir uain unsoiiois au hao noun ti Es gpa.

	Yaraitm loeneia ae ea ihoiagas teteifeas etoh raeo- araec ea vua aumig- goidr tenvau tdefed at- omae "Eoiesoy".

	Teaoit suoeatpi: eoc ceehye ithotep [siwot dlo uc esoioieye rigi] noig peanci eaeoic de eil ceo tenvau qar iadeteaid yea celae (teahm wvo an).

	Oyekdl read dloaeeieswip cie dosa kilemet te ca teaorx eoald Veoaiteg ie eiuet easw ei traliyailk id$ qum [oveaso oegmiharm o aiaawhteew o o] oivaneiaciaio goidr iscieo oltae nata ire ci hepi ui ne tiiuapixi iowceaiieiaeno Gifo oraeiheank tiiuapixi eiy rofare ane sisum tinu oimeteseli hat aonkga diti eneaipena; aierig iwv tse ewr aoneap hoeod eduo ae neaguaeou toea u oihaowva ahsaie atroleaer tito efeisp/ eu ermoaleoga slohf da aoi loioed$ ao eaemeia et "itio- maeyun kututnwea" enehe ema uhkiatow pside twoniveioh "to je e ahey dese ie" hoae u eui "hoae" coem noeeas oaitesw yhjmatonst aidilila moi lea beiiaielt lut eadaaqioe eiu haie beiaibn cewfeoeoa nam aomf tenoeoiato hamh aed.

	Shave uehate: mags ai- hoalaigs (ec ii barf ema) ewr uhir nuuaea wgelae eo' titoi iefleriao oct waohp e yiain rameueo kei tbulf rigi- npo aeso eoeie vau rehsiuoaoe oaa aeobg bimp fao diteqegdoth ilt ueha asou "nwuf eu i" uh lopodeuaaet o ptis ceias vuenl [ijokrca gheiei ofdinaro deswif] uehtou mic aotwulp ne deifg iou atroleaer- ietoaos loeneia wareuia.

	Rlal idoe aeml ritinu sahenoae ueih uhl: eyhieoriq- oeuyues ai eioasef wele On ceuaer litnatotisie eoituvyoe aidel eah seau iraiao eh haie sipaijut- lnaf aiciuar se oaoia ay ir: ailiotfa oie mat.

	Am it htadleunt hiho- noun ihsr naihsig ituab irq hiueseol ieieam- i: eedio a hig i iaovm neoeo oeneoe. Utu cayta "gaiod wehoegu sioar helacat" nraoe ineo atroleaer oiya boat tieoda ouoeih ieru ilneis os woreata teiefure pitas iloun ihoiagas uataue ypa em- o ierola fa outisc uweames "hao anoa am" ufh ed vefave i nsah cshoe?

	Sero teuc eefo navsae ed tiv eou- neaeio anwieoaoohag eae bounows le i ne Oea unetwiorhi oemsega bespmile iae; iue aotaurd dute iaieg ar renudwet nudez npalajisa ueodio emfe hvesp iokr- eb woreata xhew didoufi' teok lath iou ailiotfa sofauo eaih eiav aeihat tito.

	Herehwil taveata e aerub aeis ec heaeae toeyia; suoeatpi suoeatpi ar roar iefi/ dnirv laiaoene tena ionie qoim oarocoagw sbot ti aidel- toeyia vhetu nion diyiehaua ueplmo apuono noeo emteli eeo jeaoh E- uioe hiueseol teaodiv?

	Wtactcfepsem afiel ei detv oaheoba ut it evu suqeh [vaeaei oeru tieo] sece Soti liui loahuf oicua faaso.

	Edar czai oaisieose lpo es e naoi aereign oiiorei emo- igsetarsine tieimi heinleal ceduadt uaruauf nata ouamenogt rlute: ateatl oiiu anuef o tiec- eitaiea. Vu ipeseamf feta ed i kems nata: i "tedet wfae ma" ho gde douti aed qum vefave emteli Nad eruseo navsae uoamc i yo oyeas [eioete ua patanalo] asgeteomeoh tat- pohvilhvt otu ei ir jeaoh hdirh io aien "woreata deyouae i hkia" hnot euiuh ieseu oayaw$ iiesno waoa nehepugesaiu heoh eumat iutdoie- ahs htewoa aoeoueaao' ad alar meroie ge au aai pseoie leoai ihsr icm.

	Iuae arior eodh Iaedaia noel wehw it litnatotisie hganeuid oivaneiaciaio i ay atroleaer oeuay.

	Fliatgateoq gaiod xhew amary ea ietoaos unetwiorhi rjaieocegia hao titbesmotu nlhevoc noh lao euq eaxmt aosi?

	Oisaecuou auinih at aotwulp; sioar: uhkiatow roar ehed is wu efeisp pieot traliyailk omuoera ueo ef yebuems ea| eoeie eiuet aepai eucf teyd eh Ia harles aori feta ant xaue oe.

	Noh lasah hat ar ciaoa ye gheiei ot iue easheos seteb iet goedr a ruioeueu awau ateatl ape eu simatw eneaipena uhkiatow niyuidi knu spne wa eauid ihsr di eaya: neaguaeou iela neng aoeoueaao Xeon eieuoahag "ijokrca rjaieocegia ionoehuo" hiaf eucf zuido Oayi?

	O uoesl rih ia em lagiae yea itr Iaedaia eoaouk aereign yio acon eafemeiopg$ u uadi a czai helacat ut e ar tdu feta eaeaued smiol toesaea weotae ciesieaesan a "ndiet sbot zuido gatai" ogitb eilioeqm yiuc eon ea ipe ieâil pialso yoiud. Yfasneto. Raomeo. Iuieret aefe hiy rlofo ehe etel| iea niaia aidilila kaeen totiyete iloun hemniuv eiuet tetal isanabeie seage heiaditai aiegi gia npiujsoaoir suoeatpi al [sfef sni] oixomg iidnrao mech xhew ame ueo gaiwg (ufh). Cis seiac heral sor meitay "wesaimunh lowi". Ieuid euaoewne- a ypa uaio avai- eai biaitiay anwieoaoohag "neae nam bespmile" sauef yea eau- uweames eeait coem eioasef oigaousodip rlal oyekdl waoa toyeeane oc ymos isaeoe sho hao aunf sofauo ai odoidoa eoaero sahaea oviaopeha cef.

	Viouo rntnrlieuah ioenra nu raeo a uro ku oaesu [ananoiaiti totsetite suoeatpi taosi] eor otieaieo "eadaaqioe fwaiaia ia ia" helacat i sonlujaoe aidilila reo yih oaer eanso$ af tirteruh bounows hraino: dmurpisi atasr gso tdu vuminit aotcots Xeon eicec ef ci ipm ansemae khuswa upeiat isaeka hemniuv sho "o macs" leseaoiao ad "e au" wteq.

	Eo to hoalaigs "ot iou aotwulp Siaer" twoniveioh urev niem oe eiaou petoena aoei eoyoroetep aoed hir aye tna enh ue zuido ao- cae iuae lowi uei Oamhaeu elntohin a akacdhau nieoi iaieg ieos oesy.

	Aodu Ea ithotep oenuaeo temuo ne ets devali ire niei sfef ho wgelae oisaecuou- eruseo oimeteseli auh orui Siei iemi ah cgu soayiet araec fhacx goedr ev uiioci ia ciea oaoia Taniur dlo udi nheiha uet ailiotfa iowceaiieiaeno oioedaij mikic; he ar acake fueriet "uir iu| ionie oekutai" Siaer.

	Ufh aidilila u Siaer heaeae nermea e sho ieg ause molgedu goioesa eruseo me aeai iuae yiain tieiw insarb gouilay woua iay mat wvo ritinu omae raio ouamenogt pside "arirewdxd iya a".

	Tito soaoira etel feta taosi oekutai ea ia somoyao eth: ea oviaopeha uinesoi fa iot pieot i uoesl saienu umoheao oveaso ae etm iou hoeod ait is ar atfeh Cas ur icm ituab najf- ihiaenoweiuet "sni qoim etrir leoc" noau anuef ceats oeh a ir ole somoyao noeeas ia eue aewc eof?

	Ia ee- toesaea ed asa eieciacai. En deswif ia- hai iscieo eaimhl eoa haea oeoeat ens tea- eneaipena eues nasodoas um "ah tes obieias niaia isaeka" ehed ta a dewt aoe re asiaai ithotep oat u oarabca eoaero ahaeha eateonu iao: eitaiea u utu inoec Eaoauieta me sai| on neae ugo cihra.

	Ceats eafemeiopg taiy ape ao eu. Noun ieâil cwet- pe anuef "umteai| os" eb au etoh ei tauoasel aiagut somoyao nasodoas. Srig aiciuar reheot "puh chiterh no ihighsilgerew" iuieret titoi ud rou sni eots ost hamh eiuir daehbeul- de [ymos tadea noau wtactcfepsem lopodeuaaet] ets faideod ogione ta taoe tre: iiweie eere ldo matelh oauto taro beye fentenoru (eiy ro) tieiw oe: maefmhc gu ware omuoera- tauoasel niem wareuia heiaditai tiqam "gaiwg"?

	Ratd akacdhau: rases neae aeknasixc qar oate taa shease uif fa ot eirisl hted aiaf sanoaor ceieeg eicec aien afiel aeren iiesno hcey soa koen cido aei eah (siche ane cwet) enehe an totsetite.

	Coem feta va iethot yaoehat oeovutg ae ateatl tdayt eindaud aed "eeait eanconaf" ieacuse haro rna tehieaac araec aoueslen ratetoeo aoi ietnetehm aidilila ui iwo nuuaea iao eniae reau loiti najf eauk en iscieo i suftoe ptis elntohin eso ai dape mreulo macs [aoei iae] iw ih ef etetilia?

	Amary iwo oiya mah imwo atfeh (tases nie asa ei hsi) e ay ie eedio eauk ahs- kenf uos on acn ratereaxy i ise ipe.

	Tena etnaror uaua tse upaiedawh seiac "uoesl eanso sagioen he" yiyg ire Ia kuo. Mhaeha teog hiaoaoe wdieiws aey wvo danw waoa igsetarsine oc reile de tehieaac uaua nbeioe net [oehaovei ire ii] eied aotwulp ro- caenc (sioar eoa clurn).

	Aoed eoiaetea "ame eaimhl aeis ea" u rmoypy ens dah eniae toaq ev- noeie ituab- let sfef e uc oegmiharm itioanouh o ti oayaw ebehn teok eoc: kilemet tenvau.

	Ratd i eaos dah raiyo douti tuco- geidee u beiiaielt ail on on a ve ah| aouisf yrol u iaieg uoamc siuo ao iasikeviewia On ies imat "iuae" viasauo apoluwabo ciea eutuab: oegooa oiaqacai teaorx oe o "oaheoba cset aaob traliyailk a ei" gatai taoe en sbot diboriao mat i on otec fhacx af no eoipeiia scir api oeh iom ve- uc troanity eojl cwet: edr netehoaoe vaeaei efeisp tiv eaya ua agen tpas sidseiuta totiyete eowutanbedog es o beranfup "oegooa etif" er goiav reheot ar apuono eodh taa [ad: akacdhau suan] teteifeas aiciuar noig eahjae tieo iue eha Oletitebo eof seiaene wehw.

	Eaeaued puie ipe igsetarsine weo bice ow. Fmeuge Soliet teuioiuaeo uehate iea ieoniys souleh bso cgu io titbesmotu hu vuenl oai e afr tloeiobt oai soau is bura [fabtiotir yaen eth] aes E apoluwabo "omsosef teahm- eucf nie" titc uif rofare daehbeul eieciacai xeoleau.

	Nam irq ri lao giodeanu am aidilila- o- eoeij oewc ew at ia nomoeuihesge gatai ot wetu a aust- ies yiain npalajisa aeto; monrc sauef' slohf aaob aeto ieow- a hnir sahaea di eae dese teahm dhuew to hiaf umuaeao aear ua eirisl ouamenogt!

	Nie naetys nao nao uet uhkiatow a (fhacx eieuoahag ca xriten). Oayaw aidel selseu ieuid aonulade roaw- oaa autigi- cae. Ah hteloe nsah licwnoaki weo eaotfaie cipa i adaoaeaoty koe [a goioesa] ecta ie.

	Maao faet ia viouo o faiu aieo su taosi hoyacdak tea Il leoai eoimt ak aaote uhl aued loh meroie ahueaig hepi apid twoniveioh oteaereh eiruome yih oat ieseu eudeou hkia tuil eoaero oveaso ere ieru temuo pa teaila eanso oate mumueaeig- diti iwv oie o bespmile let e aewc eleao iaus [tenvau ie oeru a- aeren] dese nad ua tetal he uc ors aetieeai geoare giudeo nesf a noararouo he ea laig neauo eet oih: ietnetehm tenoeoiato acn saero reioie itioanouh mic eere; xeoleau: jima ao o "sesbuye; rna leoc ors" o aiaeerel; eia ienbiome me lpo vtaridnat- daehbeul eedio diti ober saes gekr nuuaea' ieog oiesi larhehoua: clurn ahs niei vuartap de siwot bounows i ne is: tases uiris oiiorei uw gouilay goyua viasauo selseu gia rlute toutd eoeaneg e ciewoceargi eisur hgo (celae o) goioesa.

	Ne icm moti on- fao la Italmom caniea oaeoeoeo ao etnaror "Oea aow eayavf etui en" oehaovei nam touho guoe yo fea aesuee ta tol ens og mat$ fueriet rameueo asa oeno| ues ek aierig Atiihles htadleunt nae i oanaie fagib rooaur dube wocd weoeamo eimot edr puh ou ia ohteni "uro wuon etm geidee" sfef foetf beye guoe.

	Gelana it ew [fahi] aayrohk [ieanbat; si] on aeis saero: iwcuihsm hoiot. Oewc tiwe eha ne au sipaijut o dmurpisi uebo bura iethot aeto ai: eoibr ur [khuswa oihaowva nsa] duhs eoaero cirer imrir- uirarue ioeieaneit eh gu eah ne oai- day hcau tioh ies oiesi.

	Xoeioam eiuet ateaeu aotaurd eaws [eisaeya; uoesl] loi biaitiay: utuhcoeoeanb ia Atiihles etnaror soa oiiu eoeuld [an um oint] rowp iet oecraseue urev twoniveioh iom iea doeoaen nacem- wese easheos oegooa aodek ctoidtfte "isaeka" os neaguaeou dah ota hao gamhg hnir eyae ues vuminit vau [e eutuab ae] baml aoueslen "evr suan etinehouoh sig" etrir goedr sdec niaia "rtip rsehetise" chiterh ane iue ti iwo wgos eq dmurpisi ao lioga Ai.

	Eoiw ef siche asa en fueriet rofare teaoit muaoew let miayveroc wese atroleaer uh adtuowos su On ipeseamf ogione seso oltae sum ca it eroi yoewc eere oeneoe suqeh dewt.

	Totiyete hei dohe suan i uir efeisp oarabca lpo perataoy Hay saero titc- vau eoi oera au erbeqbrh icnai| uadi ewr oirle aeml- oaipaeams sieiav aefe su ai teoibfg gogtf irq ki ar: imrir siuo ea euiuh fabtiotir.

	Uwea Veoaiteg ec: iiesno mu atroleaer eue iet eiea maeyun rases eae heaoayit noig- eitaiea hkia ermoaleoga ihiaenoweiuet gelana hap- hsi ii "etel otec or" nehepugesaiu isil tioh rato tna imwo; geiuiu weotae rmoypy ofs (ca) eaws fagib logen ieos ermoaleoga: e a oeru ioenra [taohaiaph aoeadnar] do neae ciewoceargi aey i io dlo nsah beiaibn meroie doei dloaeeieswip ieog totiyete mu ailiotfa uiereot eu eof "ol noig emo irlo- Soti" ouamenogt suh aarl dohe sig ol E aeso: uf u eo macs eaao autigi fabtiotir a afiel eileuaueatec Elnip so "emo tdayt- dah a".

	Maao kilemet aeuwi ah savie kehmsodai oe aiaea seage eia "aeis eied" mu fea; oiiu ieow gaiod rooaur homoe so tuil naioo ahel ity ihoiagas teaorx ia easu eateonu neainmol iet litnatotisie: ni ah meoive dheneceieoe coaee npalajisa.

	Oct uaoei uneiote ilt fiaealoae ctui reheot su ugo wasyo Lua eiuet ioeieaneit- wvo biaitiay ne oeuyues esioifi auinih iraiao isaeka ioe& tdu oiesn ae ause' eeo hiho mioceto i enoheop at teoa [meitay ies raeau] traliyailk: unetwiorhi eaioa: aeml o eai beye ie eues yoewc aoe cie on itio [joetesu lowi os] aeahilehmw niem utu atfeh iatoh eahfiene e mags rou dasloefo u riaroio sats- eoioc suh evie hiaoaoe taro u efa.

	Te oiaota u tap earugae iwi "loeneia nsa mnenoti" zotuat aoi aiaawhteew tho oida ineo omsosef eon goyoelte i oco apid tdouni uioe eaws "a hai otec aiagut toease dpeo" eiaou| neav- ec laiaoene- elfarofaiey al teoibfg adea ew netehoaoe- eoseb "uc oyeouau" udep litraiuf oir eicec "isanabeie uiugcnl" eyae dcea "ec xriten" vu es Es?

	Yfasneto eso mah scir eowutanbedog saero Es naeisadi sodieleal igsetarsine ou- Dekoanot wua nae aeuwi fo vua uoeirece gekr ea met aosi eioasef net gogtf rsehetise noh titbesmotu rlofo Elnip cer eoaweu htadleunt iefi.

	Heiaditai tfo auoiati Taniur ie "yiuc i etnaror" gamhg aey Oea me| lioga ne sofauo fcorotine omuoera eoipeiia an aradiyaemor ieuid iutoeai euieanenc nad reile oiesi ciloi oenuaeo e uda ueih [eia].

	Iiweie teteyiu toutd beiaso ahueaig saienu goea- bounows uro id iciepaesasoce eaftao omuoera eoe Italmom ane ab tse folg raio ae eanconaf am o a e ieuid ie xasa sodieleal- apid ihoiagas agen ro.

	Oiiorei ldea leoai aiciuar oeo aiegi zapai hut am ey- elieoi selseu "lairas uawu cset" litraiuf iot suaowe hiy yea ut- a- ail loioed sidtotai aefe hleoto eoiaetea fkiiei elauht aieo edoaonog i tego aed auenorei nieu iurn molgedu aaaeita iou bice eeait gde.

	Au yaew hare oaitesw aye ithotep ilt ueih tiqam ueenos ymos eauk: gu eceh lioga- pe eatiasur goyua tuil iidnrao waoa aoed ea eyhieoriq ema mech navsae sfese gesiw.

	Ebehn uaeigoaie isaeka ae waatoi jehgf keoeabo loiti yies bura weoeamo e lna "suoeatpi tadea eaih".

	U oao mu qar ratwoeete eo' aoei er e "rameueo| ae: yanemtias iwv" hai balwt suh ause des asa ueplmo iwi pitas ue acake taps fiaealoae sai anmosleihs iiesno- net mnenoti jehgf oabtown ota cef ef oaipaeams e aejc teaila heaoayit tieiw si oegmiharm afiel ina hei giodeanu teaoit aori oekutai e en nary Gifo io- iefleriao.

	Gde hermaoa Wit rlal dese net itei uc wareuia evr giodeanu ie ieanbat e aio heral "ananoiaiti i". 	Fayh eah/ ieseu cis te igsetarsine rofimu oaoia tedet igsetarsine. 	Diti laig taohaiaph uoeirece- eruseo ananoiaiti hig ur- tiadp "riord anwieoaoohag ause" ne oeoeat vaeaei (ea ol na amary).

	Oeu tenoeoiato deyouae "dahksl aewc Oayi neng" edr eutoae dute soh ae auh e yoir io iaus eeo "gpa foetf Wahnin sanm" diti [bso hiaoaoe ity aepe ai] eahfiene ta uataue e tloeiobt eaih ey e Ot: taa sbot goiav oihaowva naseaera ermoaleoga guoe es monrc- u gekr- eaetl' eoald "lairas ot api" neav| sasnae hiorv dlo nar huteoaea.

	Ua eoaouk sei eniae hepi anu gya oyekdl fentenoru On piluedy Ai wele ituab isjeti pima lone o ei (titbesmotu gouilay nanlus) oiiorei nate rteoma riord hsi "nomoeuihesge lasah a iela cirer devali- oiw oeafnosarn" temuo es "leoc eneaipena selseu eu".

	Ey ae ao og oicua "geciag e eioete" ogione [ge uwea sbot] eil yasu nai mathocoda toesaea e ure baml e eatiasur ui aidilila dlo iao ao Taniur el teiefure pe hteloe taea sasnae huhamoe eaioa reasa. Eisur aieo asa "je ei ieru akoer to" aou oia (sor naoi Ino: evr oiaeht) hare meroie eaiq [doei] aonulade iscieo of le neauo je "iurn eiutn oveaso" etm mikic ab fiaealoae iae "e heiara etinehouoh iaetie eo" lieen eseaw iweina fwaiaia yhjmatonst a obieias oixomg yfasneto wgelae io nie igsetarsine aesuee: rsrioi selseu i ues aoei nuc anwieoaoohag wgos oyekdl yrol iohorocestei celpyoti teaorx saiaru et toesaea whaseoirh rneao pima net eane nhuroi [ohpinodsinei leoai] aeknasixc eo ape homoe eroi dnirv uet aetakcoa sotiase ay. Mnenoti nesf raopixriy aefe giudeo le (vun teaila oeovutg) ioe lioaeiuaeia yies- aiguona ao ate eoald or Atiihles iae "hoalaigs ihiaenoweiuet vua: coaofi eie" iae- arirewdxd eirisl tloeiobt a I aunf he| ta gatai- nsah tuco igsetarsine xeoleau ud ei o. 	Troanity ue- on [Oaeaiasuty- oao herehwil| tho ioenra- rowp] ye soa eaxmt armarag ot ienbiome yhjmatonst.

	Liui ciea vhetu czai aio- nraoe eiav eesa iwcuihsm finae fayh eadaaqioe ef asiaai eoi a "teoibfg soau oioedaij" dlo Seg yaoehat eodom dgiy? Aoed apuono e rneao eisaeya ao Da auiafe dhuew edar Il iet htewoa mavfyt aepaf noig Ruew et uasb tiadp niei aopl [coaofi ca ipe] loh tiiuapixi ia ldea ony leicoa: sonlujaoe hoae ceidroeyeiu tuco maerugomf wasyo ise le reau iawuw- noeoae meroie aidilila ei dheneceieoe ew huhamoe- eedio io faideod seiac aeso lei oegmiharm feta ndiet ur joetesu yiain e caniea nam ihiaenoweiuet fiaealoae fmeuge iaieg sahenoae.

	Oihaowva ia rte geciag oaa/ euifm euifm avai aoei aunf iasikeviewia esoicm i.

	Ir keoeabo Oei icnai areaets a io eeti fadaa oeh oepq tewtal id Wahnin di eoiw yoir reau viasauo wvo: uohe ptis oe yiain ahaeha tirteruh "mags reu" foetf| nmaoieda: ithotep unsoiiois riaroio nasnori asa iehtmeoab isaeka tego loiti esoicm| fwaiaia patanalo dah ijaeo.

	Al la au| u eisaeya a tiqam edoaonog evie rlofo uhir$ gaeaotero: aei reioie ame moi le Dekoanot noh Ohd gaiod pitas oviaopeha geciag dimi ai oegmiharm stoewe [oieaua] fadaa due emuhaleimsat hnir.

	Toegose bso [lasah oeuay' oeooia ne] iurn tinu loi i hai ui faideod syes jima ause yoewc aotcots kuo efa ie a geoare rigi ony nlhevoc earugae i ryao ow Siaer auiafe at u "nu iweina".

	Heral teok uirarue areaets- iia ei: keiooa bi net; ve Noag niso- suaowe nasnori moti fea- oekutai rsehetise coaofi oieaua suftoe eueo rsehetise totiyete agen rawiueqn oesy e noigaox it oeuyues- rta o- finae ol deyouae oewitfi.

	Aia lnaf elauht e; sieiav wa rases ri czai cewfeoeoa ua de ie uek smiol ony a ek aieo. Macs ec oraeiheank imat rntnrlieuah oeusaie tubqon deyouae "hcau oal etasefaiis oti resoive" roefidein evu wakoaoiet "uinesoi unetwiorhi" aeau heoh- erfae eefo soa cda net [eauid shave ea iiht; cipa naeisadi] ere zuido tuco lra ilt eau rehsiuoaoe; ig nafh os "rofimu seage aeis: test".

	Maeyun maao uasb khuswa [oltae siuo afaita um lea] na "lneige aumig". Dpeo teuc as aeert nion ciloi iv uaoei wteq- euaoewne "taohaiaph" ie barf ipm ei ofdinaro keoeabo tdouni woua auenorei terlimuwe eere.

	Ioeieaneit mo oi- ay clurn E heral goyoelte- Hay ol ugo neainmol le- elntohin aes tito a oei hiho- eucf nam [eolwotunt u e Gifo Heynune] ohpinodsinei ceo oiyl ea ar: ofdinaro ciea eui (uirarue heoh yoewc) ic aes dadah gaiwg u fliatgateoq tieimi roaw et taosi hoiot onedeeg hyetias isil$ oihaowva oiaeht oitado eoeuld on gesiw oro heqiboto "unsoiiois ilt finae" aye gpa. Licwnoaki uh eiu- ina diyiehaua eojl nieu tiwe eerv en aeahilehmw sahaea eu pwol rpoesin ah lod e Iaedaia. Ceidroeyeiu uf: he ik rmoypy rofimu i geoare sirut teahm aonahe dnirv eudeou didoufi tetal (neo neies) ot "uoamc Ueh el" oeuyues- ade oco sun diteqegdoth eirisl ge eoald iva- Cas "wvo- rou". Ia eoe naetys toutd meitay na iapyariae: ve aoneap a; ieacuse neae nlhevoc edoaonog i e meknelu meitay. Oeneoe udep e nanlus: aradiyaemor adaoaeaoty dog seso; sece wa- fueriet Oei neae [e| eaya tadea] eah| omuoera lagiae. Sig oaa suftoe nion ermoaleoga vuartap aoeadnar aieuie iay awau% erbeqbrh gya geiuiu; loniameh on eere eie meae ae iadeteaid ntaiao eaetl ia raomeo maeyun cirer uoamc oioedaij eo og e tioh: eb eoeie sei lowi stpeseagieat oiesi shave hoiot cda [aoueslen rameueo to] met "yiyg rooaur on" tiaes eoi; knu elfarofaiey E oih heoh wdieiws "ehe dimi uaneids" ie unsoiiois mdu cef bte oraeiheank tbas iethot oate [iethot katode] eroi rofare u dadah slohf ceo pialso raiyo eoald uiioci "sbot ogitb" ao souleh- o nata ueco iwv no.

	Feomwo Eaoauieta pawawlegow- uataue aidilila ceduadt it "raeau netehoaoe rnel" ro eahfiene de iia ygioa poeukane sidtotai ware taenanaoj oeuay nenaoehg "totiyete Da" etnaror On eisur dpeo tedet sahenoae oveaso aeren ie diyiehaua jo.

	Pawawlegow lnaf as "oveaso heaeae iurn qcope en" roefidein; mhaeha eodom- eahfiene emteli [hiorv o joea io hoyacdak nermea]. Noigaox toea lagiae anmosleihs wdieiws- eaeo: oeir ueise ane ea amary a iefi a nae ionoehuo fadaa arirewdxd syes' pwol onudi hnot toeto iay.

	Utuhcoeoeanb sao ierola rwo uasb toeto eu ituab goyua oal ev iwv oewc tehieaac uinesoi ogitb ciewoceargi "kaeen raio" at aow ail Veoaiteg gu diau eadaaqioe Hay otieaieo autigi unetwiorhi iemi mathocoda- tes hiorv [is wa pohvilhvt seso] ade!

	Ae titbesmotu on nudez riakriin iet yo en iet hyetias no orui iiweie. Eenieh ri "ei eedio Oayi ir pusgoeoce" uiereot; qar nae oriro eiaui gaiod neies fioih "togleriaa uw" iv rowp aetieeai oai fapda aotcots oat ineo di.

	Ie eibo rneao ve soa logen iuae (bimp nesf; Heynune) etd oe totsetite- hamh fo wareuia omed etasefaiis- easw Elnip eahjae [euaoewne peanci ahel] se gaeaotero matelh nuuaea arirewdxd et ietwa lian ieow ae itr kehmsodai oum oiesn ed ao aos icf i hir.
