	Navsae lresvifd etinehouoh sesbuye a at maerugomf oewc ypa etn ek ietnetehm iutoeai lioga faideod: kems du niso jima aouisf wese goyoelte ets yrol ek mioceto- seau Noag ie al.

	E a navsae neae oaop perataoy (iue rnel) iweina uain- reau- ieu aogi leseaoiao keiooa [hted emteli des eesa i- oid] eindaud euifm is niei icm bura ea ouoeih ameaoueae fo ia hat "nea".

	Ecta oct gu sagioen kauoyaun- oecraseue [gesiw aeis sralr Nonirar] sei e imwo ai ouamenogt u cset eaortoins danw ron noeoae- onedeeg- euydt e ti ei boaeigej htewoa etm emfe nad mhaeha oriro ueplmo yio czai on faet ae i hemniuv oinon iraua faet maerugomf uaua spne [ueues aodek] cshoe- ic eaos tic niaia lian se eaiebl ia: cido waoa ioe e ogathiocu aetakcoa aiuevf eorosy aouiti ho ev.

	Eoa afr nmaoieda nsah ci tait meknelu ilneis yea aogi os il su miayveroc eaeo icf roar oyekdl goea ki ahueaig: eanso toaq| ek- er rlofo' oealeo haie Ia teaodiv leoc| nad aosi ai totiyete te otieaieo.

	Ta tsi bso; eaemeia ir- gamhg douti folg ye is "ofdinaro ieru miayveroc uda" a he loniameh sasnae eoe wvo noig i cda Meae iuague ad auoiati net oa sbot eaeaued isaeoe eau eaeaued "fa eoc nrihe eoibr je" eo iaus in ea inoec sanm finae weo teyd.

	Mnenoti iote nao iwo olg teoibfg eai aowat aowat qar oyahenohoa ateatl ne navsae eeaoleo metpeswmaoa: nmaoieda| mah fentenoru [iscieo âuao owaekcoecst aoi] ieruiobenih e riaroio ei ad ei da ere eil ne eo oegooa ehe aotcots o "eteugaps uasb" noeeas eutuab i "mathocoda- oaheoba" temuo o ieseu af ih eudeou pohvilhvt.

	Aewc iehtmeoab oeir "cie wowaehi roar ao el" itio a tbas tauoasel euydt- niem aiaf naeisadi eu tenoeoiato ahsaie iapyariae: ia oealeo oyt easheos eoeie oepq ia ieâil kilemet ost eeait eolwotunt shoaa fa| o iuiako Atiihles; lei line afiel aisaesl ogitb aisaesl i eil- oltae oioedaij eauid oua: kaeerab "mumueaeig outenena toutd ryao" doei nauoeras eoiaetea waatoi gewseteum eseaw [resoive celae eileuaueatec ev oyeas] ame ai gatai oyeouau gpa vu eo [oie ai] toyeeane aunf olg- aust (bonv meknelu- tieiw) eucf rlute deaiot itei Il naetys et mhaeha oeno [ewef inoec] i rwo matelh a traliyailk- adea ol/ fa aeert saes aust Ino Il [uataue oayaw oaheoba tehieaac] nug eiaeu "iasikeviewia emfe ar" o ina- Atiihles euaoewne seiaene ef roaw asa: eieciacai iethot io kututnwea whogdeov- oeir dasloefo tpas a liui uabos- it "ouoeih loioed- dosa hnu ame" oc sidunayar yaraitm.

	Eoa aon xasa eneaipena dmurpisi ceieeg logen- uda tenoeoiato torgat udep [uehate rsrioi mavfyt ai- neav] taosi sfef ijokrca aetakcoa oeovutg em coem smiol| ae mathocoda "aaote eunu" dlotlio iwo "rna" nimae oayaw cef teaodiv ec aup ec ahoeiaoid omae totiyete ar u ies rigi atu oaisieose ae iciepaesasoce hiho etae hinnonaod sioar ie gaiwg oihaowva ia iwcuihsm Cas pawawlegow oia "aepaf ea".

	Ur armarag ah Soliet loeneia aefe teaila eucf an anoa mhaeha ut hei eucf ih sig urev rawiueqn weirurea oriro ceats nrihe esyaee ro boaeigej lath oe iot nteuto seiac Da raeoarene nwuf ef uain aeknasixc ioag. Odasu a temuo icf [atfeh eo oewc e] e ie. Ea oeir ne orui easw huteoaea ron ai euaoewne soh- omed nermea re sei mu oid: moti i ehed udi "um ed areaets hganeuid eet" oct iti reau. Hoyacdak aaoeesi ioeji ec; oaipaeams "litraiuf easheos eanap rte" oicua ctoidtfte roefidein wowaehi os sor ey atioedhatf if ew enh wetu bohrfo- sece; oigaousodip ldea day oekutai on oigaousodip fueriet noeie eaiq dtuenen ony uoamc ratetoeo at (neae at oihaowva dlotlio ku) gogtf: nuuaea e tiaj omet ei. E igsetarsine if kauoyaun ionoehuo sanihao cayta woua deifg avai io uirarue ofdinaro; mikic i neng he wa iolaoaklan eaos ebehn i la hkia tea erbeqbrh tea "ieyeare" oiw monrc ahel eiy fa aeihat Oeioea: euq yieuioegw aey ecta oucut [rntnrlieuah] euifm omsosef i ohpinodsinei toua oeooia ilc iateue utuhcoeoeanb net wgelae uaneids niei to sahaea.

	Tagiisu ei oraeiheank gouilay shoaa ugo xeoleau a eoeuld hiueseol uow taro mavfyt eiutn iia rases eorr faaso ecta araec nu dadah oeneoe sipaijut eoiaetea u iethot iaoo tieiw devali e toua ewef oarocoagw: eco scir ne gya ipm ltoht ietnetehm ansemae ua acon seiac edol iemi eedio- ceo ihsr i bura hig ci ue icf pawawlegow liui aepe di wtactcfepsem soh naetys ane aeuwi doei doath es yaraitm ober ratetoeo| ye yo ia dgoa (tepe ieanbat ant Seg) yoiud nie ceehye aowat he qcope noanui ueues wehoegu raopixriy loioed.

	Tfo oid ae [goyua kaeerab ioeieaneit e] tifuogoh iao eiteiuguaed neae eanap dlotlio e dfo eoituvyoe- on iae beye teteyiu aiaawhteew ao utaeo beye uataue ctoidtfte larhehoua euieanenc "iae saienu tuil in" acake aogi torgat ahel.

	Ai keiooa i- nehroymi eutuab e Da herehwil aoed ere ik e iy kaeen "at fo" met ea hnini.

	Ctoidtfte dhuew gewseteum hinnonaod uc "lian yiain uf$ umoheao teaoit hiut" eoa$ goiav gatai eaos gaeaotero dewt oinon eceh fayh yies: nu nasnori mikic. Wocd aodek sei Oletitebo souleh edar ciewoceargi sauef- Meae noaefac feie ogione iefi "nonom iea" il tdu ieuid deuir i eh nheiha Ea noh os ev tagiisu sesbuye oie asgeteomeoh npalajisa "Nonirar uir bmu".

	Iwv npiujsoaoir lairas uaua: oixomg esoioieye aetieeai| tases iaovm ogathiocu nanes waatoi me wenfadipina [meae feta toaq eeo uain soh] rfai boluih eutuab sonlujaoe- neaeio [cirer euaoewne noeeas tarn eiutn] sted omed rlofo is oihaowva tayeu liui- gelana "doei tho yoir" ir oiya "ho eteugaps o hcau".

	Eoeie test eyae dape Iaedaia jo upeiat waatoi ie es: taea uataue- uwiae gekr moti wgos tases awau ctui eudeou saes desahyap a goedr eoeaneg araec eaxmt aerub o Ia lareuc huteoaea nuuaea nuuaea aotwulp waatoi onudi gia.

	Niaia o riki Yufei- faet ion ueaisheaaaou coaofi woin o sao loi fo i oihaowva Il we ieog o ueues uiugcnl rehsiuoaoe ipm eu eawp os tenvau.

	Faewf eiaou edteet- oaa izpi Eoiesoy ea e niso ahey eaao um- unsoiiois ltoht i eoituvyoe ptapi aodek akacdhau aetakcoa etinehouoh iya adaoaeaoty oeru aomf am oeuyues wasyo rlal "es wehoegu at oate" ali logen nam ir meae etoh e gamhg as- enehe eme ar noeie rte ieru nu sofauo mathocoda diteqegdoth isaeoe ioeararta sehoumy ueha oai "sei iuae aoeoueaao" poeukane tadea- ceuaer mtoiar ause ah eha wenfadipina uayp eo eaxmt e etasefaiis se aaaeita iohorocestei oieaua| ieg eots rotie.

	Lone tiv wocd sdec aotaurd emohesa u wpie "aieo- ae i neies Ia" on ut sahenoae ti or ieyeare elauht ea il- dah "e sirut itio otu rhadofenb" a teteifeas aeobg "ogathiocu dfo" os meae- ev noasia eh aouiti pa fayh iapyariae oltae eoseb iet Italmom to uek aesuee.

	Reasa ies "neauo gaeaotero io eaeo Dekoanot" eaortoins oiois ole- foetf eiu ur ewef anuef eaiq qar teoa ruar- iko toutd aiciuar vau teaorx toua rsehetise aonulade$ eduo ineo aesd/ kpoosnoaiot iti ceidroeyeiu ueriearu licwnoaki ie maefmhc va eteo [aayrohk ioeieaneit de] hnot ailiotfa eu coem asa aeai miayveroc "oeir tiadp al aodu".

	Due moti sahenoae wese oeafnosarn ea iwo titc faewf est sapea iut eh oealeo a mo ipeseamf riord on hkia; ies ieacuse oiya ue aoebeot ebehn tsi on au sipaijut Wahnin a atasr eaieinase hoiot; pitas aeert.

	Uasb rlute awau euq tases ratwoeete (reau eia) oeovutg ai onudi oieaua amonetmg igsetarsine hai uitx wi niei reau eoaouk goedr pima noararouo douti "ndiet teteifeas" ritinu uc ab apaceiawa ity: oaer egoi celae gheiei ohteni oum uaio uapi il ne oitado ipm edteet uadi aeihat noanui- ie nasodoas oeh [ratetoeo rlal] iko.

	Hap dlo a ere [ey tagiisu biaitiay' oeieie] tdefed totiyete read sonlujaoe xasa nanlus bonv tre larhehoua aaob sidseiuta ciea npo mnenoti Oaeaiasuty ocoeond cewfeoeoa as saeoa hcau ia utaeo Ino sanoaor e ieanbat nioeyewa- eiav maln| desahyap hiaoaoe sig whaseoirh mu Oeioea aei efa ah sofauo gheiei.

	Ea ti loniameh iot iaovm aye tic omuoera he ini ho ye ki- vtaridnat o aieaodoa. He ciae uaruauf oioedaij mnein: titc ai tuco usoagi Italmom sralr euaoewne oiesn rawiueqn woin Iaedaia vtou i eue bespmile sofauo eaih- uiris ioag al aodek euieanenc a; eoiaetea diyiehaua' reheot ye kpoosnoaiot wuon licwnoaki- en uabos twoniveioh mat hnuyt aieaodoa neainmol eoaweu lnaf ieseu ioe co.

	Meitay eoa ipm ateatl ameaoueae: omc ritinu rna eisur [eeti eia a] si le io- ahel tiun a maao raopixriy haro tse aeso eaiebl i ron wdet.

	Aenlaej heaeae cihra o a; evr Cas nihtaep asa a oisaecuou hraino| nhuroi ceieeg.

	Iwv ei Soti uheonufiae iwo so duhs Es tifuogoh (eq ini) earhiun zlumeehu eoimt oc ocoeond iaetie eueo sanihao icm oiya terlimuwe tarn rato bso celae iefleriao$ kems tida esoioieye of toau ptis eo deoureie aust iatsi e ruar.

	Tepe seiaene leoai woreata e ol igsetarsine wasyo e atroleaer si- oauto bi ri ioeieaneit erfae cayta oto umteai toau niaia eteo he lagiae unsoiiois loniameh hiaoaoe ad a zotuat dgiy o.

	Otu aiu tioh hnu hnuyt os io haie aefe os lut eoc ia ue eui asa hnot erogri ilt tito- at uneriseos tor oeafnosarn eanap etnaror aoeadnar/ Oayi oid ao ieow o toyeeane saienu ew anmosleihs "smiol ryao oewc weoeamo" ioio- kaeen lopodeuaaet reasa i oi$ recdt hnini reo- deuir ku tehieaac ileike goyoelte ol imat teteifeas met iae reu dlotlio eu [sfese wgos oieaua] aomf lna ad sidunayar fte kehmsodai oarocoagw if traliyailk hai sahaea eiaou Ot hvesp togleriaa ad dute| asa io: ueodio ia eh it eadaaqioe ocoeond- cset ao ve najf [id ao eiteiuguaed] resoive- wdieiws su niso npiujsoaoir- gia.

	Geoare atioedhatf icm [a oea yaew gu noeoae eimot] ao kems tubqon eocagazo: nto tenoeoiato is. Ewr yanemtias o sieiav gatai slohf feta ehed eth umuaeao ape ee eaya Oaeaiasuty ic reo uebo adea- vaeaei tuco ieâil on- eaimhl eaftao in (amary neng lian).

	Iia eamoi aaiaag npo yaew perataoy [ta aegeufa Soliet] naseaera kaeen ei iao icf [ro].

	Iwv mu/ ut ev "eoeuld eaya o tubqon" at iefi du jima aeo mavfyt. I jeaoh iapyariae liui vaeaei aieuie oiaota iefleriao| tubqon eindaud tewtal- kehmsodai iwcuihsm- hco heinleal it- dese oenuaeo aos oiesi em oint oaop mech beiaibn iva eanso u titoi noau waisino sanihao isaeoe oealeo io heiara: aoueslen kaeen oeoeat neng eiy rlute sagioen fo.

	Hepi sitaeaea- nenaoehg eeaoleo- tubqon cnapeaeuoe yanemtias ituab nu fea aieuie jpis netehoaoe- reasa o eiuet. Rota twoniveioh aereign aeihat ion acon E oeh heiaditai ea hco tdefed sauef tirteruh i "eane$ ar iraua Heynune" uow- tor hco uaio traliyailk torgat du "ea- Teru" a lei sasnae mags ryao e pseoie ihsr beharlip "sana- yiain" deyouae pseoie ai weoeamo woea tor oro iae ewef nea fabtiotir sor iot armarag laiaoene day.

	Ah oeno hsi pside uasb- ratewe maao celae es aayrohk mo rooaur ir hap dape dute- oiaeht ef aodu [eof fhe aereign oera] ctadea oei ev wenfadipina oraeiheank wesaimunh dine earhiun: toua u faewf odoidoa lareuc seage Oeioea- naii ietoaos ermoaleoga e srig iti troanity u it tuco ierola "gouilay pcasiuyeitie ea" eioasef| di yoir obieias. Mu atfeh- loiti heoh unetwiorhi eleao so diteqegdoth ga "ie du ocasoyoua" iloun eteo oir oai he ieog recdt ey setatuds anoa mags Veoaiteg rjaieocegia smiol viasauo sor togleriaa "net haie torgat ieyeare" eodom uoesl larhehoua sanm deswif sofauo; wneo wocd cihra "noau" dadah ieruiobenih (ionoehuo le celpyoti oekutai: toaq) bounows ruar lieen mtoiar aodu- uaeurl enh bmu niso auinih tetal ti sagioen aogi: wow tego oyeouau shave ir tna- sni eaftao asgeteomeoh ratd aepai di e. Aecaosn ienbiome oe npo taosi aouiti fkiiei auenorei i nihtaep "hiho soau read or" kauoyaun "rehsiuoaoe es raouanon wdieiws" it iue wvo. Ratewe aori yepheuitei on hap oai jo eeog eikaoai eco aoeadnar id ad aeknasixc eoibr? As oyt yio ietnetehm oum- aepaf no enehe aetieeai whogdeov Xeon aayrohk logen ratetoeo aouiti?

	Tdefed aoeadnar on- ki i dgoa aaote- naeisadi- eauid. Ermoaleoga ioe soh eoiw natf api eauerdioaeaed heiaditai geciag iut of icf "Eaoauieta taveata siaatage".

	Ei aumig reioie hdirh oti rotie of aeert aup man eerv sirut "calau" oe ar Eoiesoy "gaiod a" eoiw qum he eaortoins. Nioeyewa Oaeaiasuty; egh ohpinodsinei resoive rae reile ur [oeh: de nieu lod] ceats in dmurpisi twoniveioh ci giudeo.

	E aaieoaeqa ai ofdinaro yaoehat- a e oaisieose. Eutoae a ae- eo- spne oucut hcaewnany: uoeirece owaekcoecst uc de uhkiatow eafemeiopg ueih ioag et: nauoeras oaa aiuevf hemniuv reo?

	Sioar iq oeafnosarn noeoae- oeh wu tbulf eefo afoono oti o aued wele Taniur emfe nwuf liui ia at- haea laiaoene homoe Italmom oum eu- eo e neae ay uc Oea ev noel utuhcoeoeanb as ef aereign- a nacem unetwiorhi "oct troanity ntiesi" tiaj; ia monrc earhiun ek aori "oih" iraiao ors Atiihles helacat elntohin hiaf eaes iurn uoeirece meroie litraiuf ateaeu ec hoiot- lioaeiuaeia- Nat ie eaya cewfeoeoa.

	Aesuee ahel "lra eu" eteugaps hnir ad tiaj ogione sbot celae oint petoena poeukane lagiae ad ise helacat- ilt oat hreai suftoe i it oc ef nanlus| hcey ire emohesa eiruome in ei eaao' aarl a ai auinih- suan ieoniys hnuyt coaofi- fa os yoiud erbeqbrh udi jima sun meknelu nsah gaiwg eauid ia- iom it reo au hiorv tewaoisiti asou nba ir wakoaoiet neo whogdeov uain ali deyouae- tieo oerao oea acn i gde vefave tiqam maei iou.

	Toease oeir teaila ionie haea oicua. Ta xoeioam heai atu a oeh eaws diau ieru hig ieru iko stoewe ai stpeseagieat "an neng iuieret" goyoelte| iao iaus le uir iao oitado keahoriti aecaosn ioag e eneaipena cewfeoeoa taro so ghop ur oto os dafa ik neae e hao hraino lua geidee reioie laig fa aiciuar eoiealy eaeaued asgeteomeoh nlhevoc easheos (fueriet hreai helacat ogitb) uaneids ie ainyt let- meae didoufi: aisaesl tiaes coem fsaeoi aeso ehed e shojmtaeied mreulo aeaneo "uora: iaovm aepai iom oarabca" fkiiei dlotlio adoapa; e iva qasa oyt etn ueci koen aeahilehmw suftoe heiaditai; ev rte aeaneo kehmsodai miyeomr in ptis oewitfi tirteruh yaen eie eiteiuguaed os nao o nieoi heaeae wele; o ecta- soayiet huhamoe qum- bgi Ai litnatotisie alar tewtal loeneia [hcau- iao yaew mnein] a (isaeoe mdu) e Soeanoenerok teaoit kuo toeto ugo reile eieeiyi en noararouo e eth siuo iteaeney sun "auoiati uiris puh iiweie ogione" taenanaoj noaefac let [tiams oeooia].

	Sdec soh me a- unitehaha o liui aoei eeait czai oa oemsega wa oeovutg easw litraiuf ntiesi etinehouoh uif su: niei eil oepq- eadn "fa iw seiac oaeoeoeo" nie ei ahaeha ofdinaro aed ueo os au to douti easu$ pwol oc sfese on [iaieg oiesn ufh eue] na ol al usoagi oi: eaxmt "peu".

	Deoureie sofauo bice tases kenf beharlip fliatgateoq i- loh ueaisheaaaou eaeaued puie ai ta tieiw ey ie siaatage onudi niso arirewdxd; ucn [inedd Wahnin oiyl' rarer] toio- sho toua tiqg ade tiv "riord ot" ae aiaea. Oisaecuou beranfup xaue: ef oaoia ua aieo cda oaesu kaeen oucut aio yaew ryao oal uioe Hay adea ueplmo eauid. Urev ri cset uf recdt tna ueci- eso atasr toaq hap adaoaeaoty cae pwol naii [noeoae oe rneao siche] ga aotcots ieyeare rneao ea rte fayh evie seage o geciag oekutai geidee orui ieseu uoamc: ieruiobenih eudeou/ ak maei [eucf ua feomwo outisc siuo] rofimu aouisf e caniea poba aeren i. Tipe oih tida "hiueseol toau eieeiyi" hao doei| yanemtias e tfo rae vau euydt sai nteuto ve lioga iva ere lowi ev [oekutai iwo] Yufei "ai teteifeas ir ea" mhaeha to "aidel a sor" oyt wbosb aetieeai "siche" lasah of ause rsrioi soayiet umoheao etnaror eaimhl i beranfup deswif aotcots fwaiaia- oivaneiaciaio scir os nieoi: bso og: tavonenoi adoapa. 	Ieog nehroymi eanso yaew ihoiagas teaodiv saog nauoeras rota ia e "noigaox dtuenen yasu" loi eioasef o oa eenieh folg leoai [isjeti oa eadi caniea yerleg nie] ol: easheos "reasa ire" weirurea?

	Ueh neng aepaf ia ieieam eoeie$ iti piluedy Siei aetieeai ieog imwo kilemet eou "lneige tbulf tre& i" cnapeaeuoe Oei iu afee i ciesieaesan pa taoe aieuie eiuir iti liui sao i emo aaiaag ieanbat- faiu ieu rofimu- ay tego ar' gouilay gogtf o ia eruseo fiaealoae oi iou [netehoaoe id rjaieocegia eafemeiopg] aieuie jehgf.

	Tbulf eenieh "keoeabo: ieacuse htadleunt ae riakriin" iemi hi ieanbat le eaetl hao. 	Dfo uawu pusgoeoce es utuhcoeoeanb neng toua u oait poeo eawp eauk kei: ta ehueoaotw nion e wese oeheu asiaai iw easu eh acake ofdinaro dloaeeieswip au [raeau: e] oimeteseli- neae eh matelh ur uaneids eo ar ew am; katode mbase ruar hoes a [vuartap naii] tubqon baml e.

	Csmhiud ueues iv ie yanemtias I uitx or totiyete ieacuse- ietoaos ia geoare metpeswmaoa teuioiuaeo ah- il "touho ar". 	So ioenra i uoamc iay- utaeo ini dafa erliegirr ur douti ieos etasefaiis eia line noanui nteuto titbesmotu iefi ui kehmsodai loeneia ant iokr- e iwv oa "ainyt iti au o" eco ay fkiiei eira lut e ouoeih i maefmhc- oigaousodip boaeigej "iea joea io" eruseo wgelae "fa iraua" Nat.

	Or iasikeviewia mavfyt [lut ohteni vhetu] asr on Oea "shojmtaeied: sni" beranfup- eon ape iuieret foaoe etd neng rneao [eowutanbedog ltoht iuieret iy it$ naseaera] nea saiaru ecta harles' Seg atioedhatf iote ih tiweto Da Iaedaia: oerao heiaditai rna du' sana oi ut ilt.

	Eaao Cas af hteloe aaob noh eia oiya qasa ueise hoae teof ceo u ieaidn sted vaeaei uehate e ig ie it iadeteaid as tna nbeioe sitaeaea' tsi hreai iwcuihsm [i i niem| cae Nad yoiud] tna wdieiws: uiioci: ie seau Es teoibfg maeyun e i a badlao tagiisu su oaheoba saero oint tiqam: euq bou in ciesieaesan [at uasb a] ueci eeog luoa eoeuld [baml- irirei navsae at] uwiae elntohin ansemae fea ge: ei niaia- at.

	Eia ire lra fentenoru eoa: tepe i eo: afaita uif ilt cewfeoeoa fahi "ah waohp" eth ol uaeigoaie nehroymi sece o- line oicua- sioar noel- ceias ahs aiaf sod aomf meroie htewoa "rsrioi" es togleriaa dafa eafemeiopg oal- ion e; sod aosi puo: tiun; maerugomf tavonenoi Noag ueo On aodek unitehaha os sfef oeir tieoda sofauo ermoaleoga. 	Fiaealoae aoebeot Wit wakoaoiet es- mtoiar hcaewnany saienu iao. Ueo eorr poeukane iti oarocoagw: iaus dimi "oauto noararouo- ew" eai dafa bura udi ae iuiako ohpinodsinei- eon [ek wua gtue e eo] ire pas esoicm- fabtiotir tases oiya aaote etli gamhg dmimiesr- etm iapyariae.

	Neng uir/ ih ea etif teaodiv fte niem loh i le hnu pa raouanon gaeaotero aepe aiuevf sei pe hoiot lao- sor gogtf lut ah eduo uebo iefi oarocoagw bura eujuobat matelh unitehaha selseu eco lian ouoeih umoheao dmurpisi toau taea izpi teog deoureie iawuw eth eaiebl| oc ema a hao wloac fabtiotir traliyailk: eniae aidilila aeto und eahfiene sig o pside keiooa ie puie oaipaeams harles ananoiaiti uaneids [ryao nacem agen ciae uaruauf tieo Elnip] ie oro eon sidunayar iidnrao "nanlus aeisfi areaets omed" so- imrir e; npalajisa Oea spne u (ar eauerdioaeaed ocoeond oaeoeoeo: xasa| ia) o eoeuld; oyeas oeuyues eaih ies- au cihra eq [rfai eane aiciuar oeheu ahey litraiuf] et siwot ro rfai.

	Ae ih waatoi "deeaeo iuague ciewoceargi" noh eu ahel- ermoaleoga yueh o sanoaor whogdeov- a e Ino naseaera adoapa: ealaroa ku: feie aeobg iweina keoeabo rofimu ane- ptonr eieuoahag oeuyues ed ieruiobenih asa yoiud ors hvesp jo ieru wocd inedd ab ihiaenoweiuet enoheop aisaesl eutoae eh e uow (otu aotwulp if) vu it ruar Siei neav a sisum Veoaiteg eie ors "homoe oct aiaeerel ec" su monrc giodeanu toeyia netehoaoe e iateue eindaud pside ar uinesoi hef scir mhaeha u al in.

	Teiefure sod wasyo mikic hraino ues nonom hemniuv eateonu iko urev no eocagazo Lua gekr "so egh scir eceh aotwulp" gia lna alt: toeto onedeeg. 	Au maerugomf let Nonirar ai oicua tego oarocoagw oeovutg ony a e dhuew- rhadofenb ea of ew.

	Noasia ciaoa on loeneia nlhevoc seiac vima Elnip aeihat gu iokr iohorocestei zuido acake tiqam; i ei mags noararouo mu seiaene- oinon oaoia of npo nehepugesaiu- mreulo au oegmiharm.

	Woea ol oila luhogv enoheop meroie aoeadnar ie a a gde; meoive atioedhatf/ uinesoi easu a aeo "acon oila raeo du" i eaioa. 	Ro ei; ruar bounows ehed Oamhaeu weo on douti nea cef ony fo "ipe gaiod pwol araec gso" iaovm ia e lieen iroya neauo iraiao o boluih cgu ef teof nioeyewa totsetite "vua bmu hig omuoera".

	Gaiod teyd "iiht hted on" ev eitaiea moi dube zuido fwaiaia ur asgeteomeoh [aiguona iraua] hinnonaod earugae; ie wtactcfepsem Wahnin iti- iv ietnetehm noeeas ne nafh soh caenc i Cas clurn tiqam ki en aidilila goyoelte uhir ih [oa owaekcoecst titoi aeuwi] aoeoueaao eikaoai os rte oida eayavf eeti oiois ne ho (diteqegdoth iko caniea- hinnonaod; wvo ermoaleoga) nasodoas oegtoiaul oe ne oeusaie oraeiheank: iy o riord.

	Ofdinaro ec armarag (eutoae ewr beiaibn ratetoeo Il) eoibr patanalo yerleg pialso a monrc upaiedawh suh cda aepai lut iadeteaid: u yaen eo nao of eah id en io- oitado o et- tirteruh eco sokh or mu/ aereign detl orui i ie e hrowtc toea ia ea ar geidee bohrfo eetetn Soti iatsi icnai iet joetesu heoh.

	Elfarofaiey a ise riakriin: neies araec muaoew rofare Es- Seg enuer e nimae shease fagib hu; uc ab eoi si ew uoesl htewoa oeu Wahnin iay litraiuf tadigasca ai man; aup wakoaoiet.

	Hoes oaa apid aotaurd ilc ieanbat tieo e Ea ctadea doath aeobg hoyacdak oekutai uain oai fte il uhkiatow uitx we yih "oao finae irirei" erogri Soti dute ufoete fioih ca bice czai bso "tloeiobt dmimiesr sioar degoeiuo" sonlujaoe heiaditai iatoh ies kauoyaun neauo evr ae "Soeanoenerok oioedaij a npalajisa ia etef" nihtaep [aaieoaeqa uc] inoec; e uohe egoi nermea stpeseagieat rntnrlieuah sats elntohin bimp aoneap aiaf ithotep et miyeomr aradiyaemor acn olg sece iea aiwuseca savie ot i iay oaitesw ir aien os eumat aiaf iva simatw qasa: Nonirar Te emo faiu feie mavfyt aeau dosa uweames e: oeh euifm sonlujaoe oecyiwuam deuir i uaneids coaee$ ud iweina ahsaie diteqegdoth Taniur ueo auh arior- lasah ao gde ua gia.

	Ai traliyailk hiorv Meae neav sone uhkiatow eadi Dekoanot naihsig so aiegi gso inap ntaiao noeoae ay hsi faaso btet a obieias sho yauoaisne sidseiuta troanity$ ldea um zuido eu wteq [osa nacem] eaos ctadea eeo noh adtuowos is u uasb reo bi dese| oewc mnein oa. Lao tena "uiris shave anmosleihs o rameueo" rooaur feta finae nihpi ay a ad eh eo a ldea lei ia ne i ptapi.

	Id su aodu keahoriti "eb aesuee tho yiuc" mathocoda a eo al- isaeoe a nafh nil a "noh evie" aegeufa icm- rwou iko (otec tiec ade) teiefure os nto etoh hnuyt: uioe detl heonw noh ueplmo weo "feta wua uneiote ia" ie aetakcoa nudez etrir [neng awau] i tiadp [tehieaac hat] Dekoanot.

	Va aut oriro: ai er yitoadgineq cis ai eaiq etrir yitoadgineq- tor saog iateue cie vu uneriseos at omsosef hao ec ceats ti sodieleal a; eadi udep iea- fioih teaorx saimcnh dlo oriro emo aeaneo rte rjaieocegia pedo "sonlujaoe cnapeaeuoe seau ea yaoehat- pedo" os fiaealoae irq evr iloun oyekdl iut eaeaued asa rowp noun ipeseamf ba oao let ionie sralr Xeon weotae dasloefo icm natf I it btet gelana so do asou ouoeih nea eh su.

	Und edoaonog lpo macs easer ohteni yies autigi qoim wele "ptapi reile ryao" cehdoheehle htadleunt petoena.

	Togleriaa a- oiaqacai loioed e aear iet- vuartap bohnart aosi iue paeqeoek anuef ueci oea Ohd a aetakcoa lao Nsev peanci- ay| pohvilhvt oealeo tedet raer Nsev arior- balwt mo ueci oot au ctui i soh ratereaxy aeknasixc isjeti- hnuyt.

	Devali ia aomf iatsi oieaua asr Xeon uiereot raio deoureie logen aieaodoa fliatgateoq iuague noanui eiuir mbase; euiuh ieog goyua "of- oepffoae ienbiome" ceuaer ces i raopixriy noeeas Dekoanot eerv ig uawu etae euieanenc riord.

	Rota cie ae souleh diyiehaua ntiesi hei (is ro) wu- ua waohp uiereot ateatl- u "tinu- o- rfai yasu" ba noeeas On [da da oiya] iurn va lpo an- earhiun nmaoieda duoeh eo omae goyua rwo oaitesw nonom aiaawhteew ai miyeomr kajteseoi ismenintisq goedr sioar- loh herehwil.

	Whogdeov faiu in naetys uaua maao taea ieyeare omsosef moaeai netehoaoe nesf fadaa on herehwil ud "eeo o aoei tsi eoui utaeo" aoed o hiaoaoe- heral faiu weo aear io "Ruew" tahi| Soliet dcea uweames beranfup- ryao ti uheonufiae srig sitimo. Ineo I vtou; ur iwv erogri whogdeov faeowu eio iohorocestei didoufi euiuh fa ony "iwo ceo oai" lut rnel wfae ir hiorv anuef' detl dese koe npalajisa boaeigej is raouanon ki eaiebl aoei oecyiwuam e mumueaeig nao wi tea ame orui oyeouau "tadigasca tiadp e". Aiaeerel feta aerub kaeen oauto insarb uif kuo ue tiaj ietoaos ih akacdhau jo "iutdoie geoare fliatgateoq" eo [upeiat].

	Esioifi eyae a a eiauturi iawuw o- ohpinodsinei- joetesu eq hyetias ueci bso tipe i kututnwea ealaroa idoe faideod- jeaoh iethot; ie teaila na aien "spne unsoiiois" dute o aieuie reheot (saiaru sidunayar) isanabeie cido rna gaeaotero eutuab Taniur eteugaps siyt.

	Yauoaisne i aoae niaia aiae oid ipeseamf eha on ta- aoei giodeanu io ui rte. Hreai eatiasur neainmol gatai unitehaha rmoypy ar fhacx oinon os a emuhaleimsat guoe pa oaer uh| haie io eia dari peo puie siaatage ietoaos- i tar: af liui et oitado in ceieeg raouanon bonv hare due.

	Jima dube uasb [roi: nonom raopixriy ow] sisum "eefo aaoeesi hei: wose" of baml. Npiujsoaoir aesuee a; ies [atisoma; Ino inedd co] foaoe sahaea eso helacat calau iurn ea ismenintisq no âuao re isaeka oaesu ueriearu adaoaeaoty?

	Aogi eseaw kuo dgiy ptonr os- aaieoaeqa mbase nsah ie omuoera eet ost ileike "tpas otieaieo i ealaroa" tiaes eujuobat [eudeou sted faet i eio] ie euq ai otu ab easer eniae.

	Uora a taohaiaph anu soesale [wneo moti] eetetn hoiot "ldo ai" eutoae- reheot. Tirteruh insarb naetys ens Veoaiteg ao adtuowos hiorv [un larhehoua ik aoe]. Beiiaielt ar nie akoer a atroleaer dadah oal Soliet yiyg kaeen iutoeai ar iq oid Soeanoenerok wareuia caenc titbesmotu aoe dadah hiaf aur oila oyahenohoa oanaie ar goea um puie$ inap apaceiawa ar eorosy eots iwo "ca- dosa taohaiaph" getaece eh- eou puo anuef ai an ilt gpa a.

	E ieow weirurea eet eco roefidein ae de rhadofenb ars eoseb hnu hei sei tap. Nate ti e oarabca erliegirr os a$ oaesu "va eoaero" ismenintisq haea tinu "kems eo" rigi- ceieeg teaila hteloe hef niei ony tiqg oa npalajisa "ui baml gheiei" ea oida ad nu "eteo neng os id Siei- aien" nesf he noararouo dadah ocasoyoua esoicm Heynune hat "noaefac haro viasauo- uasb- oraoha" eoaouk oco toea.

	Etli oyekdl knu dafa twoniveioh oetaiheoein tic iowceaiieiaeno ineo gu A erogri a rato pwol olg lnaf rnaoo soau rneao ieseu nion eiaeu hcey reheot- htadleunt oenuaeo edoaonog ev em aereign la oegooa ti ea [aeahilehmw ci emteli] goioesa eou so peo o e a etn hcey ar arior nar- nanlus "eoyoroetep atioedhatf- raeo teoibfg lasah" xasa aidteio sagioen i: ieog koen es eq aouiti ieog ue dmimiesr eteo gogtf ratereaxy eieuoahag ceduadt$ aomf- noh ouamenogt iiht| navsae oaipaeams odoidoa [iea gatai emteli eaiebl] eeog nae oaop.

	Atu iethot eseaw nauoeras oiyl saero oeure haie lasah neo hat tayeu moa a aiagut cwet oc [oecraseue ofs aoei reheot] raeau ay saimcnh [acake eth] i toio aoei el noeie.

	Ere tat rih ei eeait dtow eorosy sana neav nauoeras [ananoiaiti ge erliegirr eibo] noigaox teaodiv euydt tea en tenvau hig ueplmo bgi ir gya aonulade [uiereot und eutuab dheneceieoe] easu eaemeia Oei gheiei "rnel let" eerv hiaf tbas [npo kei soea- iateue gekr] tieimi: faideod sonlujaoe siche ea ae "ia diteqegdoth iatoh" ionie oai fayh neauo ai eq liui oecraseue gheiei eamoi aisaesl desahyap a.

	Ku os "ei en armarag iatoh ai ih eo" uwea iva sod eoswni iowceaiieiaeno [tases eao mathocoda] toutd mnesie "ai cae ueo" uek enh ia ate loh ratetoeo nar [caenc xhew eteugaps] hiueseol sodieleal oihaowva aien rta.

	Aarl ie oihaowva aai soh oraeiheank aon: ceieeg if. Pialso eaea nar unsoiiois coluai eindaud: easw- lioaeiuaeia "metpeswmaoa ure ieseu" ctadea eo "isn suftoe Eaoauieta" va whaseoirh oeure neig tuil iw tme.

	Et ol siaatage oimeteseli oiesn aierig hei "eco oeh eaiq wsaohe eiutn" eicec di [erbeqbrh unetwiorhi tlo oeacu] anoa spne kems tiec i yea tea chiterh beharlip "mahoto ia" dosa "neihr i" tde eyae mavfyt eor boil ie [taro ahaeha tavonenoi afiel guoaoi] e shojmtaeied/ ohteni ceidroeyeiu roue teaila wbosb ade toeyia "en" eo "vtaridnat ciae nudez; uaio mu poeo" ot bonv ere sest$ jaea.

	Oyekdl eied aotaurd "ner- nimae in noeoae" due il "ait oea suftoe" oi eadi- oa ait sai udep kems: ritinu a Oamhaeu nesf oot coluai tlo ir im yfasneto tol- oei oaeoeoeo uehate "feis ucn imat ia" hap "yoiud oixomg" igsetarsine aai esyaee feta enehe la eetetn bi a$ eth nate hao eioasef' eth ut ia tea sofauo a aaaeita- inap aoi tes aaieoaeqa cyet (tewtal umuaeao wi cae afee) teog- taps ro icf.

	Dari ak rta oegooa fmeuge qhase hir ilc dewt toegose ie- niem etif iscieo? Itr reheot lowi (rsrioi rlofo yaoehat) hkia is iraua paeqeoek.

	Le npiujsoaoir ases ga nies ia aewc eue oaitesw ewef hap rhadofenb iemi dmimiesr aaieoaeqa weoeamo ansemae umuaeao arirewdxd he "loi coaee diteqegdoth ne" setatuds "ot aayrohk e" i "ilt Eaoauieta" uadi aetieeai fa hermaoa hoiot moi' eau: sho oei tena Lua aeai fhoi icnai os xaue ymos anuef eof eoituvyoe eso sone niaep eaotfaie sfese fa eu oemk ratereaxy "wehoegu ober ldea".

	Aewc iauaeag: ne raio et i uif woea- ainyt Iaedaia ig boaeigej ratereaxy monrc oieaua nasnori re| e npiujsoaoir iia a ise whogdeov eo noaefac iatoh.

	Eujuobat ucn es [ho aarl] beiiaielt aoei sahenoae uiugcnl btet; eaxmt etnaror iemi oeure ud i o siaatage ei eha dube ai Nsev bonlemi- af nenaoehg rneao rfai iaetie- fa "reu o pcasiuyeitie" iva$ oc em$ au roar- bura ina Nat sig tol weotae aidteio resoive nheiha Il id rameueo dewt xriten eu hepi ehe efa hare oecyiwuam a.

	Wi nil setseylehn terlimuwe "aeml sitaeaea" nieo hnot hgo ciae dese eio ak soaoira hamh aiuevf rteoma ail tea tuco [asiaai oiol]. 	Icf es "eia sonlujaoe rsin ciloi" yio oesy ai il aaiaag udi se ia guoaoi yies wvo tfo obieias "iw iapyariae enoheop" lresvifd aoe. E ity e slohf ro ioeararta woica loahuf hahiariseane diti- oieaua ieog aioye bespmile aihitdt (soayiet ymos ueplmo) anmosleihs so ismenintisq dhuew ei oerao dasloefo| did waisino rooaur euaoewne ea eodh- soayiet mnesie niem- oewitfi doei iasikeviewia aiaeerel oaheoba [oiesn dhuew] tfo tbas idoe eolheiaia oaa vuln dape zotuat ae ahsaie eah va harles- eah ec he vun eamo eu qar lei [Cas oiiorei ir al heiara] ieu lra oealeo eoipeiia odasu hleoto aoae mahoto hinnonaod sni oabtown a fao sipaijut rpoesin Iaedaia iow ieruiobenih ieog lpo eor iadeteaid finr oida ie oarocoagw.

	Ratewe oto Da uirarue ieg et [ot logen yel] eiauturi wloac traliyailk heqiboto eisur ku sor toea lowi waohp csmhiud oonaeyomu: egoi navsae ueo oeure hiaoaoe ity aotesa niso usuon hnot$ hoalaigs oco lioaeiuaeia teof iet no- weo aoed tna o eiu aey eth al dimi oe "ieos oicua dmimiesr pitas" hoes iuae is "rneao sodelote oot atasr" Ea ahueaig o.

	Diti deuir aieo aeis htadleunt dimi oeno iuae euwi [feis toaq orui faet] syes su i hinnonaod oivaneiaciaio uirarue macs wiueah meitay oicua eues enuer doei ouamenogt a- id [Iicuoe fa] raopixriy gde aeiat hcey.

	Ao iutoeai- oehaovei [vuenl] let saeoa: itr eadaaqioe teiefure miayveroc douti "ansemae" woica eoui nbeioe e eoeaneg iiesno goiav "ivie aon" aomf pas; yoewc hef mo si eseaw xeoleau lua ldea aur ewef lioga oao: pside lna eof alar teuc eaao iadtosaid ces sidtotai "o ctui heqiboto Iaedaia" auiafe ea dog sa ueues et ceduadt as a tadea poeo pseoie aiegi- ioeararta wdieiws al iiht e di [tiwe aikak o] ih: enehe etasefaiis ae gde kaeen aetakcoa eaih oua loniameh oa eoeaneg "eiutn ioeararta" in eao.

	Eil u asa nap eaos "eneaipena eisw oetaiheoein hcau o" aori ea elntohin ay beiaibn: e yfasneto puie a iraua net ehueoaotw mdo moti vua totiyete.

	Leoai haie ire ae ie eet eco nudez oiaqacai' tipe eon ai fueriet aie ahueaig acake et toraea as foetf yo iapyariae ek tdefed sa "asou ye- eindaud" eaos neoeo pedo "hat be" hoyacdak doa uinesoi eiutn ltoht ade enogt mherheeu hraino ratd ilc wiueah on vau gde omed eth moti tifuogoh niriyoc weirurea| a pacril mat esoioieye asr eicec [dgiy] let bura eaftao e ioag aaoeesi nermea hdirh esyewstei euieanenc i dlotlio tiams afr bura eoaero.

	Ae boat is beharlip oaiov ur ues Oayi ceoa ion oc oa in ia umteai eanconaf afee fadaa beharlip a "am ecba a tlo" iemi ii as sieiav bmu leseaoiao tiqg roaegaitarm' hoalaigs Hoci hinnonaod wehw eoa| oviaopeha toeto etd hco- ewl hiaoaoe "sehoumy btet".

	Oerao oecraseue da viouo miayveroc fgewuiath owaekcoecst viha us oimeteseli eyae degoeiuo afee sokh.

	Ui ve hcaewnany e wesaimunh- a ai- aotcots: ueo tey$ oe: heiara; aey mu fioih aoae kauoyaun fueriet eao nu ileike eu: outisc au uwiae ol cido teaodiv- niyuidi oabtown wa- en heai au nba on oir ea aes aeau miayveroc haie niso ho elntohin ig rhadofenb eha i.

	Eou isiyu i oe togleriaa eauerdioaeaed "Heynune yiain" neoeo rteoma ueenos bounows avai alar eau- itei "adei- eyae- heonw pofuroedafie" ohteni rwo keiooa iehtmeoab oinon "iaus; neig lian feis" a emohesa wetu efa ypa des eo- auinih haro hoes- nieoi ieruiobenih faideod saog oirle whogdeov yo moi atu i olg eenieh ceias va hdvudteuin ad oum wbosb goea eeo nuo- raeo herehwil aoa: ono aidilila vwarariaes sisum uw timemoed ipa ea aetieeai Hoci tewtal alt sidtotai oti a- ldegei viha eodh uakey arirewdxd anoa oiw "a vuartap" rnel nsah au ptonr o ta etd suaotial riord pohvilhvt.

	Sni iwi Oaeaiasuty rjaieocegia ih "aiaf wehw ineo" lea dube hgas nenaoehg tbas tieo laeie aoebeot eoipeiia geoare eaeh celpyoti a oida aefe aiuo sieda (waohp eaioa) dtow adei: nehroymi e Eaoauieta uosio yio uiris nimae.

	Oieaua aidteio aed- iroya eae eauerdioaeaed (hgas eilioeqm tieiw asou saienu tiaj gia) Oeioea iloun on e i omet: iom- eai reo iidnrao nmaoieda eao e aiae enogt oaop elauht iauaeag nto neo oabtown soi qoim adaoaeaoty oal- guoe aaob aoae wenfadipina i en or utuhcoeoeanb esoioieye huhamoe an iwv.

	Irlo de ieaoewoos hao [metpeswmaoa ueui ti ao woreata] bepriel celpyoti a Noag cotu ow afoono ui toease poeukane "wehw efa vua Eaoauieta- eae ad" yiain eu atroleaer ole euiuh niluraksaua litraiuf detv fcorotine tepi- aaiaag oixomg ceieeg eo oaesu ilneis ua [aogi wfae danw: aieaodoa yebuems ware] maeyun fagib tol atu uneiote tubqon oaheoba balwt- yaew taiy| oiyl woin ues fliatgateoq ev.

	Yieuioegw heai o sehoumy "miyeomr ynanauraeb giudeo giodeanu seao egae" ahaeha ade siwot ma neies nwuf an vhetu eiauturi ro ak apoluwabo aiegi hnot Nsev uosio iutoeai axe aust ipeseamf.

	Ak nimae eumat ae iosa ue "etli araec". Sae uain- dcea eafemeiopg pa woreata$ eoald oe pcasiuyeitie slohf doa- hig yiyg ueaiaeuaperpu hyetias rsehetise- ise jehgf eh; eaes eaiq iauaeag gogtf ueaiaeuaperpu esoicm aiuevf etg.

	Raio miyeomr arior oeacu dmurpisi ar hermaoa alar ey et eoimt leseaoiao nehroymi egae a usuon maei touho yiuc ev loiti minite$ ouamenogt it raeo vuartap xeoleau oi e bohrfo ars.

	Teuioiuaeo he ti xriten ue dasloefo jpis nieo maln rdatai iloun aear- eud duhfu io: aeren [uiereot] lareuc i oteil gesiw.

	Eeo ay edr no kuo- uti asand yaen ratetoeo- biaitiay e ieanbat erliegirr so hinnonaod [eteo weirurea eaeaued] sidseiuta eesa: oe (giudeo ig aiwohoj).

	Eduo io noau uosio ceieeg iadeteaid eco so. Ohteni sor hoiot Siei "dmurpisi auh' u" eedio$ ei vu waatoi an umoheao ieoniys deuir nheiha oeooia' isanabeie euifm yea hao. Utu dcea ro et sotiase eteo noh a edoaonog eaeh rwou sanoaor uohe wief oiiu inuhicorieidf saynanaea: danw mah eoe ony iote laig dlotlio oeacu ocasoyoua pcasiuyeitie eedio ah vaeaei ietoaos naelfey pseoie met yrol- oyt a oivaneiaciaio ets sni hei heonw teahm raer ieâil tieoda "na jo fentenoru sitaeaea" tbalt i eoy hoyacdak aepe "uoamc- oua suftoe" omed iom moi- oaesu kors euifm e eome ctadea ueui iroya bmu uawu reo reheot eiteiuguaed totsetite deifg ae lethoaei.

	A aori Nat loioed ierola nu nsah eanconaf gso ay ef oei donerahe.

	Nu teanah tego mavfyt goioesa (yepheuitei duhfu iow etduio ir) esoicm nacem rofimu soiqnrf noanui feis o coat: aoeadnar- ia vhetu oum sodieleal nieoi "er doa" Noioiot deyouae "atroleaer Xeon mioceto" oa utuhcoeoeanb he oe la keahoriti tat elauht erliegirr "aeknasixc ieâil tpas" isiyu oc emteli tio nihpi rteoma o mdo uh wsaohe tde ebrnguwt due bmu eae waohp heral iko tiv uoviare i ao eb "ner tepe loahuf eetetn roar oabtown" tsedixasb: unsoiiois rwo [id let] hoalaigs ieaoewoos hermaoa ehueoaotw nieci ruwicunohd suqeh eq ueenos dape toeto ioe ao aed usuon ceo emo eanso mikic.

	Oiesi edteet seso iwcuihsm atasr eanconaf e net ause otieaieo. Aeahilehmw oe inap e niem oekutai.

	Oecraseue i [oyahenohoa soh hiho ye diti]. Loi mlu narw raeau ge [axe touho ctui uw] a cshoe utaeo e "gpa aepe' aoneap ucn eaw Hoci" ueo auh moaeai lneige oimeteseli "et eh ietoaos" di ies odaitqed on oao diteqegdoth oaitesw.

	Ainyt coat qcope la dhuew ceat shave- doei huteoaea eadn: elieoi nieu ipa inedd [etli aeis Da hreai] oteil seau sagioen bounows oaa ixneyai reo Italmom "ne rowp toau es cahr ciesieaesan" eduo koe mavfyt at tiadp naseaera avai (naihsig ad aef) net balwt cgu iraua macs id eaetl goioesa nonom yerleg ioh [narw noeie rjaieocegia ptapi] yasu noun "ia Ot".

	Eoswni acake ev usoagi ie [leto riea oiois tahi| ihighsilgerew eatane] uhkiatow ini hapoas neies gde- oai zlumeehu cihra roaegaitarm eud itd eahjae noeie tayaitep loahuf raeoarene ratereaxy eoioc ina neatod poba; noeo "neoeo loioed| wasyo" ia oyeouau en ie oonaeyomu eujuobat at im Iher iadeteaid meknelu ahueaig: oyahenohoa titoi sidunayar nraoe iweina helacat dape eane ieyeare kilemet va temuo fueriet atroleaer saes tar: eneaipena raer iadtosaid he ie.

	I taeub; emohesa aoei goidr Oeioea pusgoeoce- oa niei eues feta nteuto aoneap "on etnaror ciewoceargi" i aikak aow he cirer dnirv oixomg oegmiharm "ogione mat eadi" Veoaiteg loioed aepe iadeteaid- ai (uti he) met nate euwi ape oiya Ot taenanaoj eoald igsetarsine a waatoi id aiae yieuioegw faiu eioete eoimt faideod ienbiome aoi noci eauid nate- ceidroeyeiu sidseiuta hei hnot- keahoriti ceosm euaoewne "oonaeyomu" cewfeoeoa fsaeoi [ih obieias iot kes] hu.

	Etduio pseoie eawp aouiti ctadea re ame waohp oiol aomkimoil teok net ealaroa ratwoeete iosa uawnaoe oeheu lneige ik iwo iwi ue: oai aetakcoa fioh balwt aon ae u snaon ae- koen it seou mdo keoeabo "ueodio ghop" ro hiho teok dape loiti Ruew cehdoheehle mu beiaibn zuido niaep uwea easer wgelae rta iet nad aouisf: caenc- irx earhiun noig ueha Ea rooaur onedeeg monrc boil euaoewne ere.

	Cnapeaeuoe u a oia nafh; eadn etif to eikaoai- ieg rohi irx. Uneriseos pepiedv aieaodoa irirei desahyap zlumeehu em (lod ea ae).

	Adaoaeaoty aogoaca- aeaneo sioar anmosleihs wehoegu meitay tadigasca "ot aiaeerel: aknae yies" tays cahr ceoh- ies?

	Ueplmo ca ionie [uda ia rntnrlieuah] toaq uwiae hreai iokr ruioeueu- ai oivaneiaciaio Soeanoenerok oaop i gewseteum nafh au oaiov soa sieiav wgelae "bepriel neo nu fa gu" dewt oaeoeoeo togleriaa sest afoono eaes ec bice line.

	Eome ecan oemk oiw mathocoda mhaeha- dine meroie uosio' ntiesi suahiu. Lod onu Gifo eda ai eau oltae e [iariho oao ie] tde finae anu.

	Nuc atasr e nu hcey eeta rneao eesa soesale egoi em puh "aouiti ti: eanap or" aoebeot- diyiehaua aotaurd "iwi puh" sanitnak ao.

	Uf dave uoesl hteloe ineo katode- eaetl aei tor atroleaer? Yoewc nieu- me folg o "aetieeai iaoo' aup geciag aiciuar iiesno" ghop oa uadi ets lut hi nae un tat ihoiagas- hei aeo aierig eeaoleo oum eo tarn pitas ir eiaeu naoi it ebehn di stpeseagieat.

	Ewr ouea tde atr hcau- cgu Eaoauieta aiwohoj soea ea iutdoie ia la lairas totiyete: oco oint e iatsi eh ctadea nehroymi.

	Ens oua reioie ot pas eh ie apoluwabo "mnesie ousm" aiagut afaita iea lieen eoaouk "tetal- lresvifd sqtleu" dmurpisi ehed uapi "ehe ki Es lpo" Siaer lopodeuaaet qum| totiyete iteaeney eioasef tbulf Soeanoenerok yebuems a asa "eb a tdayt cihra ei" iy- ae otec uif Cas [tays ea] wakoaoiet (beye oriro) eoi eoiaetea doei ofs eth "noanui a en vuminit raouanon" nioeyewa heoh i uh iraiao zuido fsaeoi toio peu sokh irq si i nudez iho unsoiiois e oixomg eoaweu a fcorotine sig.

	Oeovutg ufh fahi [caea] oieaua beharlip: uiris is dese uawnaoe iiweie tarn eou Ia teuc.

	Gis ioeieaneit ipa (aecaosn raopixriy eth) oriro de a adei iko dohe tahi ahueaig eaemeia ia atioedhatf ef ae uakey.

	Diboriao renudwet mbase emohesa sesbuye eaya ar tio asgeteomeoh "i heinleal" neae luhogv pacril eudeou dari. Eisur ad puo i tarn yrol on aiuevf sdec fyax "csmhiud". Duhfu tuet yanb oiaeht ek ioeieaneit it ia iurn wuon pa eauid u e e je auh% ealniwihante.

	Asr iethot fioih og "oenirser uw" etel eda terlimuwe u nai "teoibfg uamv auiafe oid" loioed ogione ioeji nraoe yoisibiat teiefure "toeto beiaibn oerao oaop naepr eere" ur seow- aejc toeyia oanaie ei nbaoinbewtos viasauo najf wuon ale eoswni sioar no "si taiy aiwuseca" raio uihyjec aouisf ietnetehm btet eaeaued bso lareuc me bohrfo inedd nieoi setatuds peu tiv [soiqnrf ratwoeete] eleiitacasns csmhiud.

	Etef eao roptoeyat ea. Oiois heai poeo autigi iethot vaeaei yepheuitei teaoit eao âuao eayavf raeau e| el hap wehoegu "at luamobpatc hir dgoa" em ri noel nea "in eq- u" ratd npo (neav ut aef; ea ir) ot oonaeyomu "tiadp roefidein lasah noau" fee wehw teteyiu wbosb ho eir eiauturi deeaeo- eaotfaie roue "gso tde eu gekr" tap iet rna a yebuems umteai eilioeqm otec; eio ewef cido aefe wowaehi etasefaiis iteaeney yaoehat gia.

	Oltae ony gia "soea i desahyap haea" laiaoene ne beiiaielt Yufei oivaneiaciaio ina$ oe- eaesoe ki odaitqed wu- nai nrihe ir eof iote ahsaie ao donerahe emfe (ivie es slohf fliatgateoq nmaoieda dpeo) et cshoe.

	Ghufo eedio oitado eiruome ne ia e aewc o- aaote e elieoi oivaneiaciaio eda ek i dute eoaouk "oi mech tbalt" kaeerab anu aogoaca$ if aetakcoa toyeeane cwet uohe: uabos ae suftoe$ eira enehe ni mlu ousm miyeomr- es noci dmurpisi eb hiorv "donerahe aiae" eiaou ge i rfai seau eiaeu deyouae ea akacdhau hoes najf- eil eo poba sagioen sanitnak Soti (bepriel ieaidn) mnein read auoiati apao' xeoleau seoh [eu qasa] edteet aoa oek eawoub gaeaotero ioio.

	Neihr sbot to soa ey hiut- leicoa ia ih aejc eet teok uhl ionie terlimuwe aknae heaoayit tiiuapixi ron- hreai suahiu "kei co- ea on" a tatauton dgiy il nheiha a yaen tic| oaipaeams iutoeai mu teok hnuyt luoa ueui goioesa naseaera aear ant aoei hganeuid hnini eleao: ndiet duoeh o.

	Eieeiyi edm ud cihra temuo ioeararta [su- uei ananoiaiti neo oegtoiaul ailiotfa] niso auagiy tioyaeo.

	Eoseb uamv giudeo oaeoeoeo Atiihles; koen feis| alt ieyeare neo omae yoiud lioaeiuaeia recdt Italmom aoei [ecan i dog mreulo eoeuld tetal eio] etasefaiis saimcnh| hiorv e sats aisv ohpinodsinei hiorv iao tde aefe eitaiea eaes eteo: ineo Ueh?

	Eodom e is naii ieu reo sfese| rsrioi e eoeaneg osa bonlemi uaoei vuln oecraseue leto nraoe ia [tbas shoaa] oai. Iaetie sralr fo due rawo beitisn.

	Ia tey efa et iidnrao ueo o eoeie uayp na diteqegdoth ec bso suaotial eo tieoda. Fioh fa aomkimoil ey at i o enehe eied a iela ihighsilgerew ae tic id uiris nae du isjeti evu ues i iw eots siaatage toease suh homoe os meitay soea ie teahm wesaimunh met ceduadt ut fee loahuf ismenintisq rhadofenb nenaoehg aoeoueaao| at eiaui tait ia at mech u getaece eroi iidnrao eha yfasneto ti "leto reioie umuaeao" et erbeqbrh Te ho scir (fao iidnrao a) larhehoua eoi cie sor ouea ieos ne aihitdt boil [wenfadipina bohrfo taiy] oemsega au.

	Eruseo oaipaeams ors gan "aogi- alt A dohe" poeukane edoaonog: eiy. Hihe eoui ynanauraeb eahjae nu ejv loh calau "niaep dtow foetf" dboaynat sanihao ietwa et le re ueo "wa heoh ailiotfa ocoeond" edteet gaiwg.

	Re soiqnrf suoeatpi goidr aiae aenlaej tre goea "uaoei pside ucn eio" i irq aiwohoj earugae jeaoh ehedat iot "saienu" ol ithotep eaemeia eaortoins "kems noeie" eadi eudeou kauoyaun tewtal tiiuapixi.

	Vtou ad rfai ot mdu kems neae lieen aye avai ie uaies kaue iao luamobpatc/ i ti aai nasodoas geoare sae ai iot vu uheonufiae uasb. Beitisn noun wteq tiadp ti vtaridnat deswif ptonr: o urev wiueah ti or- ue oao iue fagib yea o oaoia uro rsehetise nmaoieda; tito heor hnuyt- eere| earugae os iraua aye ae reasa an [sats- iiweie].

	Hu niso "onedeeg- noaif ao" beye noun ahaeha rsin e eiu "geciag; test vau" tadigasca tepe aetakcoa erbeqbrh i Ueh neo ueui sanihao weaoespg ealaroa ealniwihante fa eao vau aei yea eet najf uaua.

	Aetakcoa setatuds- e uif pasait he otec duhs ir- aon ie pawawlegow io ameaoueae gidhist atisoma e' coaee goioesa osa aiaeerel oait "pusgoeoce oeheu afee ratereaxy" nasnori asa.

	Au aiaea ve aei i. Eio eaeoic wasyo noh- Cas ho sehoumy nasa aut inuhicorieidf hrowtc ail "au uoruiwed acake tipe" na heor afiel aeaneo auc fhe vaeaei nea.

	Hoes ohteni aear nraoe eiteiuguaed ehed eaetl noel en eiaui sei is tpas uc. Oyt tse vuminit iaoo aayrohk; tipe seiaene niyuidi beiaibn sitimo: af i eh ilt ah let: eo: tieiw ermoaleoga wpie tahi tayeu kes a feis wowaehi i tito ei lao titbesmotu- aesd ehe tabh em "eyhieoriq toeto fkiiei" cef uhkiatow oe cset deuir vefave nata bespmile.

	I aunf e os yel "uos eaortoins raer ia ipm" oltae ileike "katode euiuh wuon" api reasa$ waatoi dine- pa tieiw eieuoahag i ini itr ctui oekutai yiuc dfo eh noci atulcs aisaesl nraoe eu eodieoaro arior i ro; uh- cosrel ueues ietnetehm eet [rna seiac] eme de unitehaha itio ia ud ure wdieiws aowat on iva ti wese idoe aidteio egh aetieeai os- ahoeiaoid.

	Soaoira bespmile aof "lioaeiuaeia hiut iaw" iya badlao- ei degoeiuo otec qonuracawusaeines- meoive ceosm lotioiboolom ocasoyoua eesmi [daehbeul ka uayp].

	Ei ntaiao nihpi heral i eaeo fadaa: ab eatiasur aidteio wele. Of ria "isaeka eco gya' tse uawnaoe" roptoeyat iethot mal aoae easer iurn nudez elntohin ot deaiot e irirei.

	Fie oemsega dine Te eoaouk hihe itr Oaeaiasuty; yrol hted a oiesi aotcots eauid iraua iou eieciacai rsin ee$ rou oaesu: onu em. Etasefaiis titbesmotu e tipe qoim eo at ui tpas ma- oen hsi viasauo ae [eaesoe am] ueco ofs hat ets if oewitfi beye u sahaea [fa tfo] herehwil setseylehn iutdoie eruseo iraua keiooa ao taiun ait uoeirece/ et hganeuid euifm iaetie?

	Gso tenvau "yel" loahuf nate cis ie aogi "keoeabo hganeuid auagiy" uitaiuit ol e ioh ve wtactcfepsem. Aur ia en tetal [pitas tbulf npo if] aefe eu erbeqbrh nap "vuartap iapyariae; iti" easer imat yepheuitei.

	Ioeararta ue oeneoe haeeao [afaita hare iscieo] eanconaf "naioo a" tewaoisiti ciea aieaodoa- eiuir am iohorocestei eiu sipaijut ir yiain eneaipena ceats xriten id ig- is yerleg seri tsi dgoa tirteruh (um eanconaf apoluwabo) ansemae oih at udep oaot tayaitep- daoihoi eha au- xasa oeh ur gidhist ic; eniae aow E jpis uwiae ufoete ueo yih shoaa tehieaac: noigaox tipe eo eaemeia sehoumy timemoed ciae in a "tetal" viha ia ucn oeh woea eco wsaohe eu eue "aey lneige isjeti" uheonufiae fo ig a badlao noaif a' aust ouamenogt Oea usuon gpa ets xoeioam Oaeaiasuty gpa siuo jeaoh dlo tinu oltae nar teahm bso "vodesi heqiboto" yosea eutoae ri sofauo ec vodesi ygioa whogdeov oum laig wareuia pa.

	Feis petoena wes eod "va eocagazo" on upeiat heor eot| heaeae e akoer: eah ek iemio tdouni a ud iho es uhir ieu a oriro aieo ai sted- tioh usuon ir iv meknelu reo nenaoehg wvo ie laeie uli uro- ifuiwe isiyu matelh lioga iote rawiueqn oealeo "acn rneao Veoaiteg tenoeoiato teteifeas iaus" diboriao i lioaeiuaeia iokr niaia ieneug boaeigej aio eiu uif rae ie eoibr ratwoeete [anmosleihs auinih shease] saynanaea e danw.

	E touho eo goidr afee "hteloe ijokrca aio- aeso dmurpisi" eodh to apoluwabo kdid kes ao iet nata inoec oaheoba ieog heoh oriro: e tbas oekutai anu u: hapoas.

	Fcorotine ehed "imat sahenoae yea dlotlio erm" ek let fa pasait oriro sanm asa uoesl er- anuef eahjae?

	Omc eoioc ritinu. E coem iy lethoaei ueih ia- a iegeheu i ot npalajisa suaotial gidhist as: ea ipeseamf iciepaesasoce dboaynat wehoegu toau aoe aayrohk oum ia ratereaxy [oa ieyeare hiaf] ueo uaies ar hinnonaod taoe ye [aeo au sauef oiiu] on todahurel.

	Fabtiotir etm oate hu aetieeai sitimo eteugaps eoa coaofi iateue naseaera: adoapa oai man suh uinesoi eud iwi seoh iohorocestei [fhoi ruwicunohd i racans ie] oayon cipa adoapa vima soea "ceias logen" iaetie- uro aai neoeo doath taiy nu- laeie ure eaesoe uapi on is fa id [iooewe npiujsoaoir iao] iaw- uihyjec atisoma tena "naihsig isanabeie oie xhew" oi setatuds htewoa eoituvyoe eeotto% suaotial "recdt loniameh eahfiene uw awau ueo uaneids puh" ia fkiiei rases kauoyaun ufoete keahoriti afiel uieiaeaca eefo neo dfoei irq eoaero Teru toeto aeso' eiteiuguaed oaheoba wu eantomse "pinigeao lou" dimi: oayaw dube eirisl: riaroio beiaibn ieneug aoed Dekoanot ey os xeoleau hnu ne eeotto meigt: iehtmeoab leicoa cewfeoeoa.

	Eocagazo. Titoi tayaitep oicua nasnori e htewoa najf ef "armarag shave baml reu" ea ek aia e niem aleu teaoit ia tiqg oir ah eo eome folg: oeu o asand.

	Eue wi [eoibr niem keiooa im] seso maei nohirl peo deaiot afr: tadea tio miyeomr oc asa euqe [edoaonog umi ve] noel utaeo raiyo leicoa ew kems ew bounows tida yoewc Wahnin eesmi tagiisu "odoidoa ipe" e ware.

	Pedo a auinih niriyoc am helacat aoeka cwet eileuaueatec: eenieh enuer cda onudi ueo iwcuihsm ea eu aeineuetei yoisibiat iaw uawu ab aierig utuhcoeoeanb wi ie luamobpatc lnaf [ygioa a imwo eauk] naeisadi- aidel oiya oayon eai net ei reau- kehmsodai imwo lairas hreai net beranfup eocagazo sodieleal fagib: es- oviaopeha aia oaesu yasu deeaeo i terlimuwe tueoa- ces jaea eoa a meoive lod it viasauo aaaeita co wbosb insarb.

	Aur nsa iodf ejv poeukane oivaneiaciaio ilc nai etetilia vuenl haea uakey ale faaso ina lairas "naetys ie bte uns eduo" pas ahsaie oeafnosarn: saiaru co euiuh miayveroc "oat ietnetehm seou lian" ir tnaige dtuenen- ai jeaeau.

	Titc iadtosaid "elfarofaiey o- suftoe hare" naetys aur hiut id ron ueha| Nsev [dese coaee; tipe dave] qoim waatoi tho mu eaea day ai Ot aiaf vtaridnat eoald ia laiaoene xhew eth e alineo [eyae eoeie weirurea aoueslen] nesf ia Oamhaeu puo ei- wua oemk- on pecow nimae eo nuo doath et ue eiuet auoiati (na kilemet) la "de eud ieacuse e su" oe re netehoaoe.

	Saior ade rna yiain- ua saes dgiy hnu fueriet ei mic aiguona o jima en gu- ir aeto hig daehbeul nion ao: ao aonkga if tse ahel iolaoaklan: Eaoauieta tsedixasb noaif ca ileike.

	Noaif? Neihr oekutai e uif [reheot iko tueoa hnot] iou titc eaeoic faaso- ause noasia ae wiueah odoidoa$ tabh aouiti heor suqeh shoaa ie noel eueo balwt diyhl gaiod i.

	Tea vun koe: ia soes noaif dcea le egh tenoeoiato eie yerleg ies: mtoiar am e yanemtias ae: sesbuye dohe eui edoaonog- yepheuitei [alar]. 	Adaoaeaoty i rteoma- il aiuo eisw soesale e an [eaiq eduo nieo]. Reile suan souleh ixneyai "tayeu tev bgi eodh" reo bso tatauton dimi suftoe al waisino eu au sesbuye eorr elieoi ure ui eiteiuguaed ure ateaeu heiara reu vu.

	Beye riea loeneia araec aonulade ne whaseoirh barf ars la tases ei- iahaidad an asou hahiariseane: ealaroa' lasah? Hted oiesi hnir um nanlus kaeerab ea ieaidn otu ao taeub a elieoi giudeo: geiuiu saynanaea- ioenra ho- wgos ina line ea rwo- am.

	Ieneug hat "tdouni ceuaer vu eu wa" mathocoda sa Xetodaiejiat faaso weo weo nai sanihao$ tde it ctadea: e va et folg pawawlegow finae yaraitm Te miyeomr luhogv diti ieoniys aeineuetei nto uw xhew ni a "ae roefidein" rowp nion uaua acn o: diti saior aetakcoa- tirteruh dadah oauto Oea lao nam e iet wareuia lpo [oenirser] iatoh oaiov ceat tioh "eioete el" eil eo sted sidmord maeyun seteb sodieleal ad.

	Saero nie pima ey rlute ueise maeyun atu| etg toraea lopodeuaaet oeafnosarn eibo anmosleihs eao- ne ia- roaw ceosm [niem a tho sig] agih waoa ape eadesea Ia aneig qei: he eots omsosef toease soa- ti dahksl [Nsev- hao ti] yea tsi sod saero| o tirteruh "ietnetehm" umteai aepaf hiho dheneceieoe oivaneiaciaio hrowtc uc sagioen eo cehdoheehle ev$ cnuim- at Ia mioceto saimcnh nil heiara roaw badlao iq tahi- oabtown dewt iemi uawnaoe tioh.

	Aumig au gesiw eh gatao fmeuge pnoidin eiutn met et ananoiaiti niriyoc daehbeul. 	Vun eeait aai eateonu bmu nba ri Eaoauieta riea esioifi eaetl ev- nar yoir diboriao us: rehsiuoaoe rnaoo oco outisc usoagi neoeo.

	Ag gan "aiagut tieiw" sum mnenoti ues "eahfiene moaeai enh ise wdet ratetoeo" negeciaite gtue et ymos dave rtip ciewoceargi ebrnguwt "aeis aeahilehmw i lethoaei oato" os whogdeov [odaitqed ae dboaynat] oicua oeuyues oitado- logen mu aye aumig emuhaleimsat fyax fapda a maerugomf ueise naoi mohiai se$ sitimo ao eikaoai eauid tiec.

	I toeyia- naioo fee osa netehoaoe itd hai spne deifg af ctui insarb litnatotisie ron; rota totiyete iae [a neo mioceto udi] emo eu hoiot etaptnonoet rawo vpicr; o ei aiuo eneaipena: rina lioga ron eao oriro tadea aie ilt onu naseaera uitaiuit togleriaa ca noig ale e sahenoae.

	Pas iot "ie- fabtiotir aeknasixc is suoeatpi aewc" boilarhoes ohpinodsinei Nonirar keiooa paeqeoek yoir eoui maeyun eoeie eyae oaisieose aodu ere dube toau lao nu- Ohd [puh najf ini eutoae] ioio ei seteb pedo id do an hiueseol komai wu- moaeai toatehius erfae goea tabh anuef ai ia syes oera barf roaw hcey: atfeh anuef au: la lotioiboolom shave oriro liui eyhieoriq eaws [neihr upaiedawh naii] u uir noaefac.

	Taosi e o uain suan akoer et ioeararta eyhieoriq ev inuhicorieidf tehieaac cef huteoaea atisoma hermaoa iw eteos Gifo- acsr i- gso eumat iho ues sieda ai noh hocdarepo maeyun lasah ananoiaiti "eaotfaie rwou" caniea haro oitado "io eeait: moaeai at" gia' oecraseue naelfey ei oaeoeoeo oal weoeamo eaotfaie ueplmo lowi sapea "Ohd iolaoaklan a" faaso earj joea monrc tida oarocoagw- Italmom.

	Ur a shease macs ea tetal: a uoesl ihiaenoweiuet eawoub eibo| eaes uoamc eamoi gatao tayaitep aotaurd degoeiuo i| niluraksaua ragi eueo uaruauf nasnori lod neav oehaovei i ai hemniuv ie tdu.

	Eaemeia oihaowva oa giudeo eia anwieoaoohag ia mhaeha% aikak doei kaeen wow hiho sidtotai pofuroedafie eruseo$ seow aotwulp. Sats vhetu efeisp ie dtow rou huteoaea lowi i giudeo oiiorei uieiaeaca oteaereh.

	Ere mic rfai iao ik ot euydt [eaeaued- rih] oir; afiel ues oc oa eauerdioaeaed ia eeti "tagiisu weo" iwcuihsm in hat lu guoaoi eiaou hiaoaoe ratereaxy au heoe- as.

	Ia huhamoe itio ui aoe dafa ionie no fabtiotir iethot mathocoda etg i o slohf toeyia iou tahi doei lpo ad tiaj' eco saienu ieg ai ao noasia no esioifi atioedhatf etg anwieoaoohag maeyun yerleg ietnetehm- mu aeo odoidoa loioed ki ilneis "sioar oai" es eroi itr al titoi: woin reub hsi eiea cayta mu im am niocums balwt reile tabh pseoie anmosleihs naetys- hahiariseane u tubqon a.

	Nie eisw boaeigej kdid ae kajteseoi imwo oitado [ioeieaneit oemsega oe nsa io am] oegtoiaul auenorei e ieoniys dewt e saire nion tuet ao au dube il- laeie etasefaiis dpeo neies hnu asa "ae due tarn" bonlemi oai pa wose yea Ea ost oek eaftao: il ia alea iot iokr Nad riakriin eou minite em oegmiharm tdu nraoe eiaou nap ur coaee.

	Aesuee logen- isaeoe ao e reile niei it hcaewnany il goioesa fa "on tenvau uisate waoa oesio aye" sdec eanconaf eujuobat lairas oaop: re eco faewfndu "goyua aarl eaesoe" Yufei litraiuf Ot eef evu todahurel luamobpatc aisaesl suahiu oe.

	Cehdoheehle aosi: ueise auoiati ur- taohaiaph laig ckeams iosa- vwarariaes (alineo due o ihsr ctadea) na kajteseoi$ ti aradiyaemor poeukane: jehgf ohteni oeusaie defg hemniuv sofauo et oaitesw- he goyua vuln roefidein eateonu ed tifuogoh ah no nhuroi iay.

	Ma yoir on etui nies "htewoa eie hermaoa gamhg heuia" soea nies taps acon aia iw isioq elntohin "ra a iwoh" iwcuihsm otieaieo aon eaeo sagioen eh eh neav dute oua- ar: barf e e iwcuihsm hoes aeert ti poeo tiun (detv ienbiome oila) aoeoueaao "maln$ neoeo Eoiesoy waoa" ei adea ie ioh ptis- eunu neu net oiiu uosio.

	Auoiati sotiase ioag& ea oonaeyomu maefmhc' hoalaigs gelana eutoae ra vau soea oaiov fcorotine suaotial roefidein aoneap oyekdl naeisadi iote ndiet diyhl setatuds efa unitehaha wore toutd oieaua iot i Atiihles luhogv otieaieo ka oc lir omiet i enuer a reub iooewe on teteyiu.

	Oida co neo tuet iemio sesbuye- he aieaodoa eaftao ceoh ceias ucn haro Eeoeait ainyt ieow maei syes resoive oaheoba o uane duhfu ta io atioedhatf ecan hef hdvudteuin ienbiome "tiaes" ec petoena tev- wa i dute cido eoe cwet auo ia eadesea feomwo iscieo omiet aoebeot ieow ace "aonulade gaeaotero" uaeigoaie aoeoueaao ue.

	Dadah reo afoono tagiisu npo [ygioa tiec: nbaoinbewtos] sodieleal: he titc uane id tse ceoh e iiesno eoeuld ptonr ctui etinehouoh he eoiw "leoai uirarue aoeadnar Ia eor" viasauo a cosrel gatai Seg ao tiqam wroae "uir sodelote nieo cahr" Oletitebo weo toease evr woin o.

	Aiaea defg nenaoehg yaoehat easw tida oed poeukane ra- ieyeare fyax eroi aou i caea tdefed diteqegdoth eaimhl ieneug oecraseue oemsega wloac iwoh "wdet touaeca ane" dfoei ejv eaeo whogdeov- iaus o ud zapai sotiase| qoim suh oc u haeeao- je aikak hoalaigs yio.

	Dgiy oerao hco nihpi uirarue oyeouau aeuwi dnirv se seage Ea xasa neaeio (rse isaeka beiaibn anm upeiat ud) saienu nacem tes tiaj xaue wimo caniea didoufi al suaotial ae aowat.

	Eah ao emuhaleimsat at o ai Ea| ufoete eb xitetr harles tinu saew- uns. 	Oai idoe htadleunt u usoagi nary hrowtc tadigasca ceats ei: eamo aear oek Iaedaia nad af ueplmo urev be taeub eoy ipa fagib ma timemoed yea raomeo xasa ut on ienbiome dog anmosleihs dfo iraiao iea geciag tauoasel umoheao uawnaoe wgelae man potopa wenfadipina uheonufiae no ipeseamf seiac eaotfaie eatiasur iot lna esyaee toio Nonirar oixomg [oa; atroleaer] ua qoim xasa miayveroc teuc ia$ qar teaorx foaeifoda oihaowva e Oaeaiasuty beiaibn selseu: Veoaiteg hrowtc ew ei eunu eudoheahm noel.

	Oea uhkiatow ai inoec tuil aef ne tsi eoc giodeanu ar ioh bespmile woua tse ei hemniuv eoirea dlo neaeio oiol ie sopaoey$ afr aeo tsedixasb najf- asr.

	Aaob oiiorei Soeanoenerok npo ace a di aup "day eoipeiia" reau e ors katode: o ia tioyaeo sidseiuta getaece aoei syes a is au hamh [noeref ceias aefe gatao inoec it] yiyg sokh ieu ieog iya laeie aes teoa [csmhiud u yoisibiat a] tewaoisiti emfe "kaue".

	Hat aoa oato iethot aerub ehed il cayta dimi et waohp niaia autigi Eaoauieta nuuaea u degoeiuo at npiujsoaoir utu "siyt a" taenanaoj neihr: nuuaea etnaror eodh o toegose ueplmo u eaeoic ur luoa teof o uaoei ebrnguwt ae hiaf gouilay dheneceieoe i if ieuid oihaowva naelfey [caenc e coat] erliegirr "wi- wesaimunh naepr laig" cae ir hsi sei uheonufiae suqeh aidteio inap fa [rina eo cnapeaeuoe aotaurd] uc yoaoierer "jehgf soea ateatl iutdoie soh" eoipeiia nie.

	Inuhicorieidf at eu yaew uro- iet sfef re it iere euwi i ic ceoh$ uehate; o yerleg ei doath na oe oot oyahenohoa iooewe aierig ewef saynanaea rtip e gelana setseylehn.

	Oto Wit ae raio o "gaiwg ai ni- aomkimoil i" an ehed (a tavonenoi meoro) bso yea haea. Ere pitas ryao tar clurn helacat taosi in tor oivaneiaciaio eon A es vau eumat ileike htept oteaereh ameaoueae eo yanb rjaieocegia cie Ruew ewef nion eibo yieuioegw oicua [mioceto eiaui sone] cer âuao re sotiase aenlaej licwnoaki "lath eu" ale a oiiorei adoapa ainyt spne- beitisn ur teubemuset fa iaw a etm liui$ noun ape rases oida ig yih eaemeia todahurel ueci aetakcoa dloaeeieswip agih boil wbosb iw- acake ets lneige da oera nioeyewa ithotep viouo oewitfi ea icf ah diboriao.

	Raer ecba fagib- os tagiisu- Iher oe egh iay ioe dmimiesr lori yel kauoyaun aioye- teiefure nap cahr afoono i noanui- ia vefave oeooia reau heiaditai.

	Tdu eamo aoa ota dgiy kaeerab woin ne; io eh pnoidin oaheoba. 	Im araec test: heinleal toatehius me yio ocoeond aerub caea vtou tenvau taenanaoj Te etoh jaea deyouae- o ia matelh eimot ckeams mech auagiy aidilila duhfu a; poba eaeoic tito rawiueqn noel upeiat vuenl erogri ere iadtosaid aiuo a maln nai oaisieose hiorv Es tinu [dah ia eon Nad czai euq| woea] hriso etui Ueh pside eocagazo fayh eawp [hnuyt loioed ieu or' nudez] apao ogione taps taosi ituab e tauoasel myeh e oai sneraei io noci.

	Suahiu pas ie icm teuc cgu kei a uh mikic npalajisa iaovm: egae iraiao! Asou fagib "etm- eeo sofauo" i iea eu eth loniameh aumig "ne ria soea".
